syAdetat.h | kvachidbhAvo visheShyo vishiShyAkArashchAbhAvo dR^ishyate | yathA ghaTo na jAnAti prakR^itirna kartrIti | kvachichchAbhAvo visheShyo vishiShyAkArAshcha bhAvaH pratIyate | abhAvo.asti | abhAvaH prameya iti | nacha vidhiniShedhAtmanorbhAvAbhAvayorabhedo yujyate | tatkathaM visheShyAbhinnaM vishiShyamuchyata ityata Aha- bhAvo hIti ||
kvachidityanuvartate | yo bhAvaH sa eva kvachidabhAvo bhavati | yashchAbhAvaH sa eva kvachidbhAvo bhavatItyetadubhayaM prasiddhamevetyarthaH | vAkyArthadvayaprasiddhidyotanArthaM hishabdadvayam.h | tatkathamityata Aha- abhAvasya cheti ||
asti tAvadidaM yadabhAvasyApi bhAvA dharmAH syustathA teShAM cha bhAvAnAM cha te.abhAvA dharmAH syuriti | akhilA iti bahutvopalakShaNam.h | etadapi nAN^gIkaromItyata Aha- pratyakSheti ||
pratyakShagrahaNamupalakShaNArtham.h | yasmAdabhAvasyApi bhAvA dharmAH santi bhAvasya chAbhAvA ityetatsarvaM pratyakShAdipramANataH siddham.h | ato na vArayituM shakyam.h |
astvabhAvabhAvayorbhAvAbhAvadharmavattvam.h | tathA.api bhAvasyAbhAvatvamabhAvasya cha bhAvatvaM kvachidastItyatra kimAyAtamityata Aha- sarva iti ||
yato.abhAvAbhAvayorbhAvAbhAvadharmavattvaM siddham.h | siddhashcha dharmadharmiNorabhedatvena kAraNatvena sarve bhAvAH padArthA abhAvAshcha bhavanti | abhAvashcha sarve padArthA bhAvA bhavantItyuktamupapannamityarthaH |

niShedhasya buddheriti sAmAnAdhikaraNyam.h | paro bhAvaH | yadyapyeSho.arthaH prAgevoktastathA.api prasaN^gAtpunaH smArita ityadoShaH |

evamabhAvayorbhAvAbhAvAtmakatvaM sAmAnyataH prasAdhya prakR^ite yojayati- astIti ||

siddhamiti sheShaH | bhAvAbhAvayorvisheShyavishiShyayoraikyaM pratyakShAdipramANasiddhaM natu ghaTatadabhAvayoH | ato nAtiprasaN^ga ityarthaH | yadvA bhAvAbhAvayordharmadharmibhAvo dharmadharmiNoshcha abhedaH prAmANika ityetatkiM bhAvAbhAvayorvisheShyavishiShyayoraikyasyopapAdakaM kiMvA sambhAvanAhetuH | Adye tUkto.atiprasaN^gaH | dvitIye sAdhakaM vAchyamityatredamuktam.h | anena kvachidityuktaM vivR^itaM bhavati |

syAdetat.h | anyonyAbhAvasya bhAvadharmatve.api tasya bhAvAtpR^ithaktvena kathaM bhAvasyApyabhAvatvamuchyate | anyonyAbhAvasya bhedatvAdbhedasya cha svarUpatvAN^gIkArAditi chenna | svarUpabhedasyAnyonyAbhAvAtiriktatvAt.h | yachchoktamabhAve.api pR^ithaktvamastIti tadasat.h | pramANAbhAvAt.h | svarUpabhedenaivAsaN^karopapatteH | pR^ithaktvasya cha svarUpabhedAtiriktatvAdityata Aha- anyonyeti ||
pR^ithak.h pR^ithagvibhinnAnItyarthaH | chashabdo dUShaNAntarasuchchayArthaH | gataM prAgeva nirAkR^itam.h | anena punaruktidoShaH parihR^ito bhavati |
kathaM kalpanAgauravAdikamityata Aha- paryAyatveneti ||
kramaprayojyatvenetyarthaH | sarva eva laukikA vaidikAshcha |
atra mAyAvAdinashchodayanti | svarUpabhedAnatiriktayoranyonyAbhAvapR^ithaktvayorbhAvAbhAvadharmatvopalambhAtsarvapadArthAnAmapi bhAvAbhAvAtmatAsiddhiriti yaduktaM tadayuktam.h | bhedasya vastusvarUpatvAnupapatteH | tathAhi | bhedastAvadvidAraNAtmA | bhidirvidAraNa iti vidAraNArthabhididhAturUpatvAdbhedashabdasya | tasya cha vidAraNAtmano bhAvasvabhAvatve tasyApi vidAraNaM syAt.h | tathA tadekadeshAnAmapi bhedaH svabhAva iti tatrApa vidAraNaM bhavedityanena krameNa sarvashUnyatA syAt.h |
kiJNcha bhedasya vastusvarUpatve na tatraikatA samaveyAt.h | abhedaikArthasamavAyinyA ekatAyA bhedena virodhAt.h | ekatvAbhAve.anekatvamapi na syAt.h | tatsamAhararUpatvAt.h tatkAryatvAdvA tasya | ekatvAnekatvavikalaM cha shUnyamevApadyate | 
api cha yadi bhedo vastusvarUpaM syAttadA pratiyogyanapekShaH prasajyeta | svarUpasyAnapekShatvAt.h | nahi ghaTAtpaTasya bheda itivat.h ghaTAtpaTa iti pratItirasti | ghaTo bhinno ghaTasya bheda iti visheShaNavisheShyabhAvasambandhapratibhAso.api bhedasya vastusvarUpatve dugharTaH syAt.h | nahi svayameva svasya visheShaNaM sambandhi vA bhavati | saMshayaviparyayau chaivamuchChidyeyAtam.h | bhedAgrahanimittarau hi tau bhavataH | tatra yadi dharmiNamavagAhya tau bhavatastadA tatsvabhAvabhUto bhedo.api gR^ihIta iti kva tayoravakAshaH | na chennirviShayatvAtsutarAm.h | yadi chAsmadayaM bhinna iti pratiyogighaTitatayA pratIyamAno bhedo vastunaH svarUpaM syAt.h | tadA tasya saparikarasya bhedasya svarUpe.antarbhAvAtpratiyogino.api svarUpatayA nimajjanAdadvaitamatameva paryavasyediti |
tAnapAkaroti- bhedasyeti ||
tushabdaH prakR^itAdvaisheShikAdervyavachChindanye tviti sambaddhayate | svarUpatve bhedyavastusvarUpatve | shUnyatAM sarvasyApIti sheShaH | chashabdaH pUvaroktadUShaNasamuchchayArthaH | adbhutA AshcharyAH | na laukikeShvevaMvidhA dR^ishyante nApi parIkShakeShviti yAvat.h | tatkathamityataH shUnyatApattiM tAvannirAkaroti- yata iti || yo bhedo yasya svarUpamiShyate taM bhedaM prati tato.anyasyaiva vastunaH pratiyogitvamiShyate yatastasmAdadbhutAsta iti sambandhaH | 
anyasya pratiyogitve.api kathamuktadoShaparihAra ityata Aha- pratiyogino hIti ||
hishabdaH pUrvavaddhetau | ayamityevambhAvasya pratyakShAdisiddhatAM sUchayati | svasmAt.h dharmisvarUpAt.h | idamuktaM bhavati | vidAraNAtmA hi bhedo yasya yatastaM tato vidArayet.h | natu yaM kamapi yataH kutashchit.h | na(hi)cha ghaTasvarUpasya bhedasya ghaTa eva pratiyogI yena svasminvidAraNaM syAt.h | kintu ghaTAdaya eva | tato vidAraNaM tu nAniShyam.h | tasya shUnyatAnApAdakatvAditi |
kiJNcha bhidyate.aneneti yadi bhedashabdaH karaNasAdhano bhavet.h tadA bhedaH kamapi vidArayet.h | bhAvasAdhanatvAN^gIkArAt.h | ato.abhyupagamyaiva karaNasAdhanatAmayaM parihAraH abhihita ityAshayavAnAha- kathaJNchaneti || idamuditamiti sheShaH |

nahyekatA.anekate svarUpeNa viruddhe | ekasyaiva ghaTasyAnyApekShayA.anekatvadarshanAt.h | kintu yadapekShayA.anekastadapekShayaivaika iti viruddham.h | tatra ghaTasya parasmAtpratiyogina eva bheda iti | tadapekShayaivAnekatvaM svApekShayA tvekatvamiti ko virodhaH | api chaikatvAnekatvayoH sAmAnAdhikaraNyaM vA viruddhaM dharmadharmibhAvo vA | Adye naikatAyA bhedena virodhaH | bhedasya svarUpatvenaikatAsAmAnAdhikaraNyAbhAvAt.h | na dvitIyaH | ekaM dvitvamiti darshanAt.h | ekatvAnekatvAbhAve.api shUnyatvaM kutaH |

nanUktamatra bhedashabdAdeva bhedasya vidAraNAtmakatvamavagamyate | sa hi bhiderdhAto rUpam.h | sa cha vidAraNArthatayA vyAkhyAta iti | atrotraram.h | yadA bhididhAturvidAraNArtho vivakShitastadA bhedashabdo vibhAgAkhyaguNavAchako na tvanyonyAbhAvalakShaNabhedavAchaka iti | etaduktaM bhavati | "kriyAvAchitvamAkhyAtumekaiko.arthaH pradarshitaH | prayogato.anugantavyA anekAtharA hi dhAtavaH' iti vachanAdbhidirvibhAgavachano.anyatvavachanashcha | bhinno ghaTa ityukte sphuTita iti gamyate | bhinnaM gaganaM ghaTAdityanyaditi vij~nAyate | tatra vibhAgo vidAraNAtmA nAnyatvam.h | tadeva chAtra prakR^itaM na vibhAga ityanyatAlakShaNasya bhedasya vastusvarUpatve vidAraNaprasaN^genAtyalpatApAdanamapyasaN^gatameva, ChalatvAditi |

AsyasyetyAsyasambandhinoroShThayorgrahaNam.h | tasya cha mAyAvAdina eva | yadA hi mAyAvAdI niruttaratayA tUShNImAste tadA tadIyayoroShThayorvidAraNalakShaNavibhAgAbhAve.apyoShThau bhinnAvanyonyAbhAvalakShaNabhedavantau bhavata eva | yadabhAve cha yadasti tattato.anyaditi cha prasiddhameva | ato vibhAgAdbhedo.arthAntarameveti j~nAyate | tasya chetyanena nAtaH paraM svarUpabhede kAchidanupapattiH sambhAvitA.astIti sUchitam.h | nanu kathaM nAsti | visheShaNavisheShyabhAvAnupapattyAderaparihR^itatvAditi chenna | svarUpatve.api visheShabalena visheShaNavisheShyabhAvasambandhAvabhAsopapatteH | anyathA.a.anandaM brahma AnandaM brahmaNa ityAderanupapattiprasaN^gAt.h | saMshayaviparyayAnupapattirapi nAsti | savisheShatvena j~nAtAj~nAtatvopapatteH | anyathA.a.atmasvarUpe svayaMprakAshamAne tatsvarUpamAtrANAmadvitIyatvAnandatvAdInAmapi prakAshanIyamAnna jAtu kasyachitsaMshayaviparyayau syAtAm.h | avidyAvashAttatra tatheti chet.h | atrApi sAdR^i(shyAdiva)shyavashAttatheti santoShyavyam.h | 
yachchAdvaitaparyavasAnamuktam.h | tatkuta iti vaktavyam.h | yadi manyeta yathA hi lambakarNa Agato, nIlamAnIyatAmityAdau parikaravato yadbhavati tatparikarasyApi, tathA pratiyogighaTitasya bhedasya dharmisvarUpatve pratiyogino.api ta(tra nima)nnimajjanaM syAditi tatra kiM sambhAvanayedamuchyate uta vyAptyA | nAdyaH | prashithilamUlatvAt.h | na dvitIyaH | chitragurAnIyatAM kAshInivAsI samAgata ityAdau tadabhAvAt.h | pAramArthikIM dR^iShyimavalambamAnasya tadapi asiddhamiti chet.h | aho pakShapAto.asya 
yatparasyAniShyaM prasaJNjayanvyAptigrahaNAya laukikaM dR^iShyAntaM bahumanyate vyabhichAre tu tatrodAste | parasiddhena parasyaivAniShyApAdanamiti chet.h | tarhi mUlashaithilyamapi paraH svasiddhena pratipatsyate | vaichityaM kinnimittamiti chet.h | vyAvartakatvamAtreNa pratiyoginAmupayogAditi brUmaH |

nanvevaMvidhaM mataM siddhAntaviruddhatvAtsUtrakR^itA kuto.atra na nirAkR^itamityetadanena parihriyate | upekShitaH sUtrakAreNeti sheShaH |

Ishvaro.aShyaguNatvena aShyAveva guNA asya santItyevaMrUpeNa, na prameyo na pratipattavyaH | kutaH apramitatvataH aShyaguNatve pramANAbhAvAt.h | kintvamandasadAnandasyandyanantaguNArNavaH prameyaH | arNava ivArNavaH, kShIrArNavaH sudhAsyandI bhavati | ayaJNchAnalpavidoShAnandasudhAsyandI | so.anantA guNAH shubhapadArthAshchintAmaNiprabhR^itayo.asminnityanantaguNaH | ayamapyAnandAdayo.anantA guNA asminnityanantaguNaH | amandasadAnandasyandI chAsAvanantaguNashchAsAvarNavashcheti vigrahaH | 
aShyaguNatvavadanantaguNatve.apIshvarasya pramANaM nAstItyata Aha- mayIti ||

tattadviShayatA ghaTAdiviShayatA, vidhIyate astitvenAN^gIkriyate | mA bhUttattadviShayatvamityata uktam.h- sArvaj~nArthamiti || upalakShaNaM chaitat.h | sarvakartR^itvAdyarthaM chetyapi draShyavyam.h | atrAnantavisheShA iti yathAgamasiddhoktiH | vastutastu yadi Ishvaraj~nAnAdi nirvisheShaM syAttadA tattadviShayatvaM na syAt.h | tadA cha tasya sArvaj~nAdikaM na syAt.h | sarvaviShayaj~nAnavAnhi sarvaj~no nAma | tathA sarvakAryotpattiviShayechChAprayatnavAnsarvakartA | sarvakAryavinAshaviShayechChAdimAMshcha sarvasaMhartA | aN^gIkR^itaM cha sArvaj~nAdi pareNa parameshvarasya | atastadarthaM j~nAnAdestattadviShayatayA bhAvyam.h | kathaM cha tathA sati nirvisheShatvamiti |

svaj~nAnAdhigamAbhAvAdityarthaH | ekameva hIshvaraj~nAnaM tachcha svavyatiriktameva viShayIkaroti na tu svarUpamiti kathamIshvaraH sarvaj~naH syAditi |

tathA.apIshvarasyAsArvaj~naM tajj~nAnasya vA svaprakAshatvaM duShpariharamityAshayavAnuttaramAha- eSha eveti ||
AstAM tAvatsajAtIyAtmavisheShaguNayaugapadyAnupapattiH | j~nAnadvayavAnahaM, j~nAnadvayena sarvaj~no.asmi, idaM me j~nAnametajj~nAnaviShayaM etachchaitadviShayamityAdireSha evArtha IshvareNa j~nAyate na vA | neti pakShe tasya sArvaj~naM na syAt.h | Adye kimetayoranyatareNota j~nAnAntareNa |

Ishvarasya hi "AnandaM brahmaNo vidvAn.h' ityAdishruteH sukhitve.api nopAdhimattvam.h | kasyApyAtmaduHkhitechChA.abhAvAdata etadupAdhervyApyAbhimatavyApakatvaM nivAyarte | yadyapyayaM niyamo na darshanamAtreNa siddhayati | atiprasaN^gAt.h | niyAmakaM tu nAstIti vaktuM shakyate | tathA.api shrutyarthaparityAgaM vArayituM prasaN^gApAdanAyedamuditamiti draShyavyam.h | bhavedetadyadyAnandashrutiH sukhavAdinI syAnna chaitadasti | tasyA duHkhAbhAvaparatvAditi chet.h | kiM bAdhakAdiyaM shrutiH svArthAtprachyAvyate utaivameva | na tAvad.hdvitIyaH | duHkhAbhAvashruterapyanyathayituM shakyatvena tarkasyeShyApattitApatteH | Adye na tAvatpratyakShamAgamo vA bAdhako.asti | tataH sukhitve duHkhitvaprasaN^go vA nirduHkhatvAnumAnaM vA bAdhakamiti vAchyam.h | tadubhayamapi vyaptibalapravR^ittaM vA syAtsahadarshanamAtrabalapravR^ittaM vA | nAdyaH | itaretarAshrayatvaprasaN^gAt.h | siddhe hi shruteH svArthaprachyAvane tarkAnumAnayorvyAptisiddhistatsiddhau cha shruteH svArthAtprachyAvanasiddhiriti |
nanvetadbhavatAmapi samAnam.h | shruteH svArthaparatve tarkAnumAnayorvyAptibhaN^gaH, sati cha tasmin.h shruteH svArthaparatvamiti | maivam.h | yataH pratItArthaparityAga eva bAdhakamapekShate | na svArthaparatvaM, bAdhakAbhAvam.h | tasya pratItyaiva siddhatvAt.h | dvitIye tvatiprasaN^gaH syAdityAha- saheti ||

JOSHI-1
A bhUt.h shrutirapramANaM, mA cha bhUdanumAnabAdhayA.arthAntaraparA, tathA.apyanumAnasya bAdhikA kutaH, pratirodhikA tu bhavedityata Aha- Ishasyeti ||
anumayeti shrutivyatiriktapramANopalakShaNam.h | dharmipramA dharmigrAhakaM pramANam.h | anumAnaM hi pramANAntareNa siddhe dharmiNi pravartate nAnyathA | atra cheshvaro dharmI na chAsAvanumAnena siddhayatIti samarthitaM prAk.h | pratyakShAdyaviShayatvaM tu parasyApi sammatam.h | tataH parisheShAt.h shrutireva dharmiNaH parameshvarasya grAhiketyeShyavyam.h | tathAchAnenAnumAnena shrutiprAmANyamanumatam.h | anyathA svasyAnutthAnaprasaN^gAt.h | sA chopajIvyA shrutirIshvaramAnandavantamAchaShye | tatastadvirodhAdanumAnamapramANameva | agnisvarUpagrAhakapratyakShaviruddhatachChaityAnumAnavaditi | nacha vAchyaM yaH sarvaj~na ityAdivAkyamanumAnasyopajIvyaM nAnandavAdIti | sarvasyApi vedasyaikavAkyatvenArdha(ja)charatIyAyogAt.h | anyathA.agnigrAhakamevopajIvyam.h | natu tadauShNyagrAhakamityapi syAt.h |
anenaiva nyAyeneshvarasya vigraharAhityAdyanumAnamapi sarvaM shrutiviruddhatvAdapramANamevetyAshayavAnupasaMharati- tasmAditi ||
atra IshvaravAkye | ata eva sarvaguNaiH pUrNa ityuktam.h  anyathA.a.anandavAnityavakShyat.h | 
anupapattyantaraM vaisheShikAdidarshane darshayan.h "nityameva cha bhAvAt.h' iti sUtraM vyAkhyAti- nityechChatvAditi ||
vaisheShikAdayo hi kAlavisheShe dvayaNukAdiprakrameNa mahAbhUtasR^iShyimabhyupagachChanti | tattadIyaprakriyAparyAlochanAyAM nopapadyate | kintu tatpakShe kAryaM sadA bhavet.h | yadA.abhilaShyate tataH prAgapi bhavet.h | kutaH | kAraNasAmagrIsampattinibandhano hi kAryotpatteH kAlaniyamaH | tatrAdisR^iShyau paramANavaH samavAyikAraNabhUtAstAvatsadA vidyante | nimittakAraNaM cheshvarechChA nityaiva | tathA kAlo di(kcha)k.h | yadyapyadR^iShyaM dharmAdharmasamAkhyAtaM na nityaM tathA.api pralaye.astItyaN^gIkriyata eva | vR^ittilAbhastadA nAstIti chenna | tasyApIshvarechChAdikAraNakasya tadbhAve.abhAvAnupapatteH | ata eva paramANusaMyogasyAsamavAyikAraNasyAbhAvAnna sadA sR^i(sadAdisR^i)(mahadAdisR^i)Shyiriti nirastam.h | saMyogAnutpAdasyApyanupapatteH | tadasamavAyikAraNakarmAbhAvAditi chenna | tadanutpAdasyApyayogAt.h | nachAto.anyadvayaNukAdeH kAraNamasti | yadvaikalyAdabhilaShitasamayAtprAk.h kAryAbhAvo bhavet.h | satyAM chAbhimatasAmagyrAM kAryAnudaye pashchAdapi notpadyeta | niyAmakAbhAvAditi | sadAtvaM sadAtatvanam.h | bhAvAt.h pralaye.apIti sheShaH | evashabdasya sadaiveti sambandhaH | kAryaM bhavediti chAbhyupagamyoktam.h | vastutastu tatpakShe kadA.api dvayaNukAdyutpattirna sambhavati | vinAshakAraNasyeshvarechChAdeH sadAtanatvena satpratipakShatvAt.h | kAryotpattisahakR^itameveshvarechChAdikaM vinAshakAraNamityaN^gIkAre.apyutpattyanantarameva vinAshaH prasajyeteti | ata eva sR^iShyayAdIti vakShyati | 
syAdevaM yadi kAlamAtraM sR^iShyervA saMhArasya vA kAraNaM syAt.h | nachaivam.h | kintu kAlavisheSha evAtastadbhAvAbhAvAbhyAM sR^iShyisaMhAraniyamo ghaTate | tathA neshvarechChAmAtraM sR^iShyayAdihetuH kintu tadvisheSha eva tatastadbhAvAbhAvaprayuktA sR^iShyayAdivyavasthA syAditi chenna | kiM kAladeshAderaupAdhiko bhedaH, kiMvA svAbhAvikaH | nAdyaH | nirastatvAt.h | dvitIye tvapasiddhAnta ityAha- nahIti ||
hishabdena "AkAshakAladishAmekaikatvAt.h' ityAditadvAkyaM smArayati | kAletIshvarechChAyA apyupalakShaNam.h | 
nanvidaM dUShaNaM bhavatAmapi samAnam.h | tathAhi | mahadAdyupAdAnakAraNaM prakR^itirnityaiva | tathA nimittakAraNamIshvarechChAkAlAdikamapi | tadeva cha pralayakAraNam.h | ataH sR^iShyipralayasamayaniyamo bhavatAmapi durghaTa ityata Aha- asmanmata iti ||
yadyapyasmanmate harerichChA sadAtanA | prakR^ityAdyupalakShaNametat.h | tathA.api visheShakAla evaitasya mahadAdeH sR^iShyayAdi bhavatIti yojanA | asmAbhiH kAle svabhAvata eva bhedo.abhyupagamyate | tathA cha kAlavisheShasyaiva sR^iShyiM saMhAraM cha kAraNatvAttadbhAvAbhAvAbhyAM satsvapItarakAraNeShu sR^iShyayAdisamayaniyamo yujyata iti bhAvaH | 
nanu kAlavisheSha iti vAchyam.h | maivam.h | vishiShyata iti visheShaH, sa chAsau kAlashcheti vigrahagrahaNAt.h | nanu sadAtanIti bhavitavyam.h | maivam.h | nAyaM TyuT.hyuloranyarataH pratyayaH | kintu bha(bhA)vArthe tanapratyayo.ayam.h | athavA taneti tanote rUpametat.h | 
nanu te kAlabhedA yadi nityAstadA sa prasaN^gastadavasthaH | vyarthashcha kAlabhedAbhyupagamaH | anityatve tatkAraNaM vAchyamiti chet.h | satyam.h | upAdAnaM tu prakR^itireva | nimittamAha- visheShAshcheti ||
na kevalaM mahadAdi kintu kAlasya visheShAshcha kShaNalavAdayaH | evashabdasya harereveti sambandhaH | sadetyanena na yugapatsarvakShaNasR^iShyiryena teShAmapi kShaNikatvaM syAt.h | kintu nirantarapravAhatayetyuktaM bhavati |
nanu kAlavisheShANAM parameshvarAjjanma kutaH pramANAtsiddhamityata Aha- sarva iti || 
"sarve nimeShA jaj~nire vidyutaH puruShAdadhi' iti shrutireva kAlavisheShANAmIshvarAjjanimAha hi ityarthaH | visheShaNadyotata iti 
vidyuttasmAtparamapuruShAtsarve nimeShAH kAlabhedA adhijaj~nire yatAsvaM jAyanta iti | nanveShA shrutiH kAlopAdhInAmIshvarAjjananamAha, natu kAlasya | tathA sati kAShThAkalAmuhartAshchetyuttaravAkyasya paunaruktyaprasaN^gAt.h | nahi sarvanimeShAtiriktaM kAShThAkalAdikamasti | upAdhayastu nimeShAdirUpAH pR^ithageveti na tatra punaruktidoSha ityata uktam.h- sAdaramiti || yatsarvanimeShajanmAbhidhAya punaH kAShThAdijanmAbhidhatte tadAdarArthamityato na punaruktidoShaH | upAdhibhedastu nopapadyata ityuktameveti | 
nanu nimeShAdishabdA akShipakShmasaMyogAdivAchino na sAkShAtkAlAbhidhAyinaH | ato neyaM shrutirvyaktaM kAlasyaiveshvarAjjanma pratipAdayitumalamityato.atra spaShyAM shrutiM chAha- udIrayatIti ||
"so.antaHsharIre.arpitabhUtasUkShmaH kAlAtmikAM shaktimudIrayANaH' iti asya Ishvarasya vAgapi kAlasyeshvarAdutpattimAhetyarthaH | kAlAtmikAM kAlAkhyAM sahakArishaktimudIrayANo janayannityarthaH | atra kAlashabdAdIshvarasya jagatsR^iShyau shaktitvAbhidhAnAchcha nArthAntarakalpanAvakAshaH | 
syAdetat.h | kAlastAvatsarvotpattimatAM nimittam.h | nacha kAlasyotpattau kAlAntaramasti | tatkathaM tasyopapattiH | pUrvakAlaH parakAlasya nimittamiti chenna | idAnIM jAtastadAnIM jAta ityadhikaraNatayA kAlasya kAraNatAvadhAraNAt.h | adhikaraNasya kAryotpattisamAnakAlInatAyA gehe jAto goShThe jAta ityAdau nishchitatvAdityata Aha- kAlasyeti ||
kAlasyotpattyaN^gIkAre na kevalaM sAdhakasadbhAvaH | kintu kashchana virodho.api nAstIti yojanA | etachcha prapaJNchayiShyate |

astu tarhyubhayasvabhAvaM kAraNamiti tR^itIyaH pakSha iti chenna | virodhenaikasyApyajananaprasaN^gAt.h | avirodhe tvAha- ata iti ||
prakR^itapakShadvayaM samAhR^ityAta iti parAmR^ishati | aniyatyA ghaTo ghaTasyaiva nIlonIlasyaiveti niyatiM vinA | yatkiJNchit.h ghaTAdikaM nIlAdikaM vA | yasya kasyApi ghaTAderaghaTAdernIlAderanIlAdeshcha | kAraNaM syAt.h | ghaTakShaNasyobhayavidhakAryajananasvabhAvatve.asau tadubhayaM janayet.h | tathA chopalabhyeteti yAvat.h | kechididaM vAkyaM pUrvavAkyasheShatayA vyAchakShate | sarvasho.api kAryANAM samAnarUpatvaM na syAt.h | kintu visadR^ishakAryajananasvabhAvatvAdghaTAdikaM gajAdeH kAraNaM syAditi |
na chaturthaH | arthakriyArahitasyAsattvaprApteH | arthakriyAkAritvaM sattvamiti (hi)saugatAH | 
nanu cha kAryajananamAtraM vastunaH svabhAva ityaN^gIkumaro na tUkteShu kamapi pakShamityata Aha- ata iti || buddhisthamimaM kalpamata iti parAmR^ishati | atiprasaN^gastu na tirohitaH | 
syAdetat.h | yathA bhavanmate pramAjananasvabhAvatve.apIndriyAderdoShasahakArivashAdapramAjananam.h, tathA kAraNasya sadR^ishakAryajanakatve.apyadR^iShyAdisahakArisAmarthyAtkadAchidvisadR^ishakAryajananaM bhaviShyati | yadvA yathA sAN^khayAnAmindriyAdIni pramA.apramAjananasvabhAvAni | tatrApramApratipakShANAM guNAnAmupanipAte pramAmevopajanayanti, pramApratipakShANAM doShANAmupanipAte tvapramAm.h, tathA kAraNasyobhayasvabhAvatve.apyadR^iShyAdivashAttadanyatarajanmopapatsyate | athavA yathA naiyAyikAdInAmindriyAdIni j~nAnamAtrajananasvabhAvAni | guNAdisahakAryupanipAtena pramAdyu(tpa)papattiH, tathA kAraNaM kAryajananasvabhAvameva | adR^iShyAdisahakArisamavadhAnAt.h (tu) tatsadR^ishaM visadR^ishaM vA janayiShyatItyata Aha- adR^iShyamapIti || 
atrAdR^iShyagrahaNamupalakShaNam.h (sahakArimAtrasya) |
adR^iShyamapi visheShasya, Adye visadR^ishakAryajanakatvasya dvitIy.anyatarapratibandhasya, tR^itIye tUbhayajanakatvasyApAdaM kuta ityekaM vAkyam.h | tathAhi | pUrvapUrvatarAdyadR^iShyakShaNAvisheShAnApAdakAstadApAdakA vA | Adye tvasyAdR^iShyakShaNasya visheShApAdakatvaM na siddhayati | kAraNAbhAvAt.h | visheShAnApAdakAdR^iShyakShaNAjanyo.apya(yama)dR^iShyakShaNaH sahakArivashAdvisheShamApAdayiShyatIti chenna | tatsahakAriNyapyasya sAmyAt.h | (a)tatrApi sahakAryanatrAnusaraNe gauravamiti |
tasyaiva kAraNasya visheShApAdakaM kuta ityaparaM vAkyam.h | tathAhi | visheShApavAdakamapyadR^iShyaM kiM vivakShitasyaiva kAraNasya visheShamApAdayati, kAraNamAtrasya vA | nAdyaH | niyAmakayoH kAraNaj~nApakayorabhAvAditi | yebhya indriyAnAlamabanaviralaparamANubhyastadAlambanamilitaparamANUtpattirAshAsyate | yatashchArthAnadhipaterindriyAdarthAdhipatIndriyasya | yasmAchcha samudAyaj~nAnarahitAdAtmanastadvadAtmotpAdaH | tadidaM tasyaivetyuchyate | 
ubhaya(trApi dvi)tra dvitIyau kalpau dUShayati- yasyeti ||
atrApi yatkiJNchidadR^iShyaM vishaShamupapAdayedityekaM vAkyam.h | yadi pUvarpUrvatarAdyadR^iShyasyApyasti visheShApAdakatvaM tarhi tadapi pUvarpUrvatarAdiparamANvAdau visheShamApAdayedeva | samarthasya kShepAnabhyupagamAt.h | tathAcha samudAyapratIteH samayaniyamo na syAditi | 
yasya kasyApi visheShamupapAdayediti dvitIyam.h | yadi kAraNamAtrasya visheShApAdakamadR^iShyamaN^gIkriyate tadA sarveShAmapi kAraNAnAM visheShamupapAditam.h | tathAcha ghaTaparamANumelane sarveShAmapi melanaM syAt.h | natu kutrApyabhilaShitaparamANvavasthAnaM bhavet.h | nacha yugapatsarvasamudAyo dR^ishyata iti |
JOSHI-2
tha matam.h | sarvamidaM svavyAhatam.h | tathAhi | tantavo yadi sadR^ishakAryajananasvabhAvAstadA tantvantarameva janayeyurna tu paTam.h | yadi cha visadR^ishakAryajananasvabhAvAstadA na tebhyaH pArthivapaTasyotpattiH syAt.h | kintu pAthasIyaM kimapi jAyeta | ubhayasvabhAvatvaM tu viruddham.h | anubhayasvabhAvatve paTasyApyanutpattiH | sahakArivashAdvayavasthAN^gIkAre sahakAriShvapIdaM samAnam.h | athochyeta | asti(stu)tAvattantupaTayoH kAryakAraNabhAvaH | pramitasyApanhavAnarhatvAt.h | sa cha yathA yathopapadyate tathA tathA kalpayiShyata iti | samametatsamApItyata Aha- kAyarM cheti ||
nityavinAshitva itayetadvakShyamANamatrApi sambaddhayate | yatkiJNchinnIlAdikaM yasya kasyachideva pItAdeH kAryaM syAt.h | 
yatkiJNchitpItAdikaM yasya kasyachideva nIlAdeH kAraNaM syAt.h | kutaH | nIlA nIlasyaiva kAryaM syAt.h na pItasya | nIlameva nIlasya kAraNaM na pItami(tyatra)tiniyAmakAbhAvAditi yojanA | chashabdau mithaH samuchchaye | 
etaduktaM bhavati | sambhavati sthiravAde parihAro.ayam.h | yadyatra samavetaM yadyenAkAreNa pariNataM vA tattasya kAraNaM kAryaM cheti niyAmakasadbhAvena kAyarkAraNabhAvAvadhAraNe sati tadupapAdakakalpanopapatteH | kShaNabhaN^gunaye tu pUrvottarakShaNayorniranvayavinAshotpAdayoH kAyarkAraNabhAvAvadhAraNopAya eva nAsti | samavAyapariNAmayorabhAvAt.h | tathAcha kasya balAdupapAdakaM kalpayiShyata iti |
samavAyapariNAmayArabhAve.api yadyadapekShayA pUrvabhAvi tadeva tasya kAraNam.h | yachcha yadapekShayA pashchAdbhAvi tadeva tasya kAryamityavadhAraNopapatterniyAmakAbhAvo.asiddha ityataH kAryaniyamaM tAvannirAkaroti- idamasyaiveti ||
idaM nIlama(sya nIla) syaiva kAraNam.h, na tu pItasya, ityevaM nIlasya nIlakAryatvaM, nityavinAshitve niranvayavinAshotpAdapakShe, kena mAnena na kenApi | pashchAdbhAvamAtrasya nI(lasyeva pItasyApi)lApekShayeva pItApekShayA.api sattvAditi bhAvaH | sAdeshyaM sArUpyaM vA niyAmakamiti chenna | viralaparamANubhyo militAnAM militebhyashcha viralAnAmutpattyaN^gIkArAt.h | kAraNaniyamamapyapAkaroti- idaM neti ||
idaM nIlamamuShmAtpItAnna jAyate kintu nIlAdevetyatra nIlasya kAraNatvAvadhAraNe.api, kAraNaM pramANaM, nAsti | nIlasyeva pItasyapi nIlApekShayA pUrvabhAvitAyAH sattvAditi bhAvaH | 
nanu yathA bhavatAM samavAyapariNAmayorabhAve.api kuvindapaTayoH kAryakAraNabhAvAvadhAraNaM tathA mamApi bhaviShyatItyata Aha- idamasyeti || nityavinAshitve Atmana iti sheShaH | yujyate.asmAkaM nimittakAraNakAryayostadbhAvAvadhAraNamanyatrAnupakShINAnvayavyatirekAbhyAm.h | natu parasya | asmAbhiranvayavyatirekAnusandhAturAtmanaH sthAyitvAbhyupagamAt.h | pareNa(cha) kShaNikatAsvIkArAt.h | nahi tathAvidho.anvayavyatirekayoranyatrAnupakShayasya chAvadhR^iterIShya iti bhAvaH | yojanA tu pUrvavadeva | 
evaM samudAyaM nirAkR^itya sarvasya kShaNikatAmadhunA pramANAbhAvena tadvirodhena chApAkartumuttaro granthaH | tathAhi | na kevalaM samudAyo nopapadyate | kinnAma sarvasya kShaNikatA cha | tatra pramANAbhAvAt.h | nanu pratyakShaM kShaNikatAmarthAnAmavagamayati | taddhi vartamAnamAtragocharamarthasya vatarmAnakShaNamAtrasambandhinIM sattAmavagAhate | na pUrvottarakShaNasambandhanImapi | tatkathaM kShaNikatvamarthAnAmaprAmANikamiti | uchyate | kimidaM kShaNikatvaM nAma | kiM kShaNasambandhisattvam.h | kiMvA kShaNamAtra evotpattinAshavattvam.h | yadvA kShaNAntarAsambandhitve satyekakShaNasambandhitvam.h | AdyastviShya eva | sthAyino.apyarthasyaikakShaNasattAsvIkArAt.h | dvitIyatR^itIyau dUShayati- vinAsheti || 
anekapadArthasambandhitvena bahuvachanam.h | chashabdastR^itIyapakShasamuchchayArthaH | evashabdasya naiveti sambandhaH | sadAtanAH pratikShaNabhAvinyaH | pratyakShaM khalvarthAnAM vatarmAnakAlasattAmavagAhate na punaH kShaNamAtrabhAvinAvutpattivinAshAvapi | nApi kShaNAntarasambandhitvam.h | tathAcha kathaM tena kShaNikatA siddhayediti | 
nanu cha pratyakShaM pUrvottarakShaNavatirtvamapyarthasya gR^ihNAti na vA | nAdyaH | vartamAnamAtragrAhitvAt.h | dvitIye tu pratyakShAnupalambhena parvottarakShaNayorasattvasiddheH kShaNikataiva si(dhyediti)ddheti chet.h | dvitIyaM tAvadurarIkumarH | nachaivaM kShaNikatAsiddhiH | yogyAnupalambhasyaivAsattvagamakatvAt.h | nacha pUrvottarakAlavartinA pratyakShayogyA | vatarmAnamAtragrAhitAyAH pareNaivoktatvAt.h | astu vA.a.adyaH pakShaH | kasyAchitpratyakShasya vartamAnamAtragrAhitve.api tadevedamiti pratyabhij~nAnalakShaNasya tadabhAvAdityAshayenAha- dR^ishyata iti ||
viShayIkriyata ityarthaH | tR^itIyArthe tasiH | ekasyaivAnekakShaNasambandhitvaM sthiratvam.h | etena na kevalaM pratyakShaM kShaNikatAM na gocharayati | kintu sthAyi(tAM)tvamapi gocharayatItyapIti vadatA parapakShe pramANavirodhaH svapakShe pramANasadbhAvashchodito bhavati |
anena "anusmR^iteshcha' iti sUtraM kR^itavyAkhyAnaM veditavyam.h | sarvavastuShvityanena saugatAnAM pratyabhij~nAnirAkaraNaM vaisheShikAdimatameva spR^ishati na tvasmanmatamiti sUchayati |
tathAhi | kimanayA pratyabhij~nayA nityatvenAbhyupagateShu paramANvAdiShu sthiratvaM sAdhyate kiMvA ghaTAdiShu | nAdyaH | teShAmatIndriyatvena pratyabhij~nApratyakShagocharatvasyAbhyupagantumashakyatvAt.h | na dvitIyaH | ghaTAdiShu pareNApi pratyabhij~nAyA 
bhrAntitvasya svIkAryatvAt.h | yadA hi ghaTAdau sUchyagrAdinaiko.api paramANurapaiti tadA naShyavyameva tadArabdhena dvayaNukena | vibhAgenAsamavAyikAraNasya saMyogasya naShyatvAt.h | dvayaNukanAshe samavAyikAraNanAshAttyaNukanAsha ityanena krameNa ghaTanAsho.apyavashyambhAvI | nacha paramANuH pratyakSho yena tadapagamAnapagamau pratyakSheNa shakyanishchayau | nacha vAchyaM nibiDAvayaveShu sphaTikAdiShu pratyabhij~nayA sthiratvaM setsyatIti | tatrApi paramANvapagamAbhAvasya pratyakSheNa nishchetumashakyatvAt.h | nibiDAvayavatvaM cha na vibhAgAyogyAvayavatvam.h | vibhAgasya pratyakShasiddhatvAt.h | kintu ghaTAdito.apyutkR^iShyakAraNApekShatvam.h | nacha tadvisheShAbhAvaH shakyo.asmAbhiravagantum.h | dR^ishyate hi kAlataH sphaTikAdAvapi gurutvApakarShaH | nachAvayavAnapagame sa sambhavatIti | nApi guNAdau sthAyitvaM pratyabhij~nayA siddhayati | tasyApi kasyachidatIndriyatvAt.h | kasyachidghaTAditulyatvAt.h sAmAnyAdikaM tu svarUpato nAstyeva | sattve.api rUpAdisamAnameveti shaN^kitaprAmANyaM pratyabhij~nAnaM na kutrApi sthairyasiddhau pramANayituM yuktamiti |
atrochyate | syAdayaM doShaH paramANvArambhavAdinAm.h | na pariNAmavAdinAmasmAkam.h | tadeva (hi) vastvavayavopachayApachayAbhyAmanyathA vikriyate | na punaranyadeva bhavatIti hi pariNAmavAdino manyante  ataH pratyakShayogyeShu sarvavastuShu pratyabhij~nayA sthiratvagrahaNaM yuktameveti | 
nanu bhavanmate.api pratyabhij~nA (bhrama eva) bhrAntireva | pariNAmavAde pUrvottaravastunorbhedAbhedAN^gIkArAt.h | tadevedamiti cha pratyabhij~nayA.atyantAbhedasyAvagAhanAt.h | uchyate | yadA tu (yadi hi) pUrvottarakAlabhAvinorabhedaH pratyabhij~nAviShayo.aN^gIkriyate | tadA sAvadhAraNasya pratyabhij~nAnasya bhramatve.api tadidamiti tu na bhramaH | tenaiva cha sthAyitvasi(ddhi)ddheH | yadA tu kAlAdidvayasambandho viShayastadA sAvadhAraNamapi na bhrama iti |
nanvidaM pratyabhij~nAnaM parilUnapunarjAtakuntalApAdAviva bhrAntaM kinna syAditi chet.h (na) | bAdhakAbhAvAt.h | evameva bhrA(nta)ntitvAbhyupagame nIlAdipratyayAnAmapi tathAtvApatte(tvaprApte)H | nacha pratyakShaM bAdhakamityuktam.h | 
pratyakShasyAbAdhakatve.apyanumAnaM bAdhakaM bhaviShyatIti shaN^kate- phalAdInAmiti || 
Adipadena dehadIpAdigrahaNam.h | visheSheNa parimANabhedena, kShaNikatvaM (tAvat.h)anumIyata iti sambandhaH | tatastaddR^iShyAntena sarvatra phalAdivyatirikte.api vastuni sattvena hetunA paJNchaskandhA ityanumAnaM sthiratvaviShayapratyabhij~nAyA bAdhakaM bhaviShyati | nacha phalAdidR^iShyAntaH sAdhyavikalaH | yadviruddhaparimANaM tannAnA dR^iShyaM yathA ghaTapaTau, viruddhaparimANaM cha phalAdikaM pUrvottarakShaNayoH, ityanumAnena phalAdInAM kShaNikatAsiddheriti | pariharati- AkAshasyeti || avisheShataH pUrvottara(kShaNa)yobharedarahitatvataH, avisheShaH pUrvottarakShaNayorbhedarAhityam.h | akhilasyApi vipratipannasya | idamuktaM bhavati | yatsattadakShaNikam.h yathA.a.akAsham.h | sachcha nIlAdIti pratyanumAnapratiruddhatvenAnumAnasyAbhAsatvAnna pratyabhij~nAbAdhakatvaM sambhavatIti | nachAkAshadR^iShyAntaH sAdhyavikalaH | "AkAsho dvau nirodhau cha nityaM trayamasaMskR^itam.h' itrata pareNaivAN^gIkR^itatvAt.h kShaNikatAsAdhakasya parimANabhedAderAkAshe.abhAvAchcha | tadidamu(mapyu)ktaM avisheShataH parimANabhedAdirahitatvata iti |
yadvA.a.akAshasyAvisheShataH parimANabhedarahitatvataH | taddR^iShyAntenAkhilasyApi phalAderavisheShaH pUrvottarakAlayoH parimANabhedAbhAvaH sattvAt.h kiM nAnumIyata iti yojanA | etaduktaM bhavati | nAnumAnaM pratyabhij~nAyA bAdhakaM bhavitumarhati | anumAnasya pratyakShato dubarlatvena tadbAdhyatvAt.h | anyathA phalAdikaM parimANabhedarahitaM sattvAdAkAshavadityapyanumAnaprasaN^gAt.h | nahyatra pratyakShAdibAdhaM vinA kashchiddoSho.asti | tathAcha taddR^iShyAnte kShaNikatvasAdhakasyAsiddhatvAtsAdhyavikalatA syAt.h | tataH pratyakShavirodhenaivAsyAnumAnasyAprAmANyam.h | anyathA.anyonyAshraya(tA)prasaN^ga ityeva vaktavyam.h | tachcha samaM prakR^ite.apIti | etena "AkAshe chAvisheShAt.h' iti sUtraM vyAkhyAtaM bhavati | tadanena kShaNikatva(tA)sAdhakAnumAnasya satpratipakShatvaM bAdhitaviShayatvaM cha vadatA.a.akAshe.a(nA)naikAntyamapi sUchitam.h | bhavadanumAnasyApi phalAdinA.anaikAntyamiti chenna | tatrApi kShaNikatAbhAvasya vakShyamANatvAt.h (iti) | 
bhavedidaM yadyAkAshasya sattvaM syAt.h | nachaitadasti | mUrtAbhAvatvAdAkAshasya | bhAvatvaM hi sattvamatra vivakShitam.h | sasvarUpatve.api vA sattve, abhAvo niHsvarUpa ityaN^gIkR^itamityAshaN^kayAha- yadIti || 
yadyAkAshasya sattvaM nAstItyaN^.hgIkR^itya pratyanumAne.atiprasaN^gAnumAne cha dR^iShyAntasya sAdhanavaikalyaM svAnumAnasyAnaikAntikatvAbhAvashchochyate | tadA dehAdiShu sattvaM kuta eva siddhamiti brUmaH | tathAcha parakIyasyApi dR^iShyAntasya sAdhanavaikalyaM syAt.h | yadi cha vidhimukhapratyayavedyatvAddehAdInAM bhAvatvaM pramAviShayatvAtsattvaM chochyate | tadA.a.akAshe.api 
samAnamiti |
pramANAntareNAkAshasyAbhAvatvaM vArayitumupodghAtamAha- sa dharmIti ||
yatrAbhAvaH sa dharmI | yasyAbhAvaH sa pratiyogI | tadubhayavattvamabhAvasya niyAmakaM vyApakam.h | yo.abhAvaH sa sarvo.api dharmipratiyogisahita eva | yathA ghaTAdyabhAvaH | sa hi bhUtalAdidharmiNA ghaTAdipratiyoginA chopeta eveti | 
nanvidamanupapannam.h | abhAvasya hi dharmipratiyogisAhityaniyamaH kiM deshataH syAt.h, kiMvA kAlataH | Adye dharmiNA sAdeshyaM tAvannAsti | bhUtalasya svAshraye, abhAvasya tu bhUtale vR^itteH | pratiyoginA tu viruddhameva | dvitIyastu yadyapi dharmiNA kathaJNchitsyAt.h | tathA.api pratiyoginA nAstyeva | prAgabhAvapradhvaMsAbhAvayoH pratiyogibhinnakAlatvaniyamAdityAshaN^kAM pariharannabhAvasya dharmipratiyogisAhityavyAptatvamupapAdayati- tau vineti ||
atra dR^iShya iti prakaraNAttau vineti tajj~nAnaM vinetyatharH | chashabdo.abhAvo dR^ishyamAno dharmipratiyogipratItAveva dR^ishyata ityanvayasamuchchayArthaH | hishabdenAnvayavyatirekayoH prasiddhatvaM sUchayati | tadanenAnvayavyatirekAbhyAmabhAvapratIterdharmipratiyogipratItipUrvakatayA vyAptirupapAditA bhavati | yadvA tAvi(ti)tyanena na j~nAnamupalakShaNIyam.h | abhAvaH pratIyamAno dharmipratiyogighaTita evAtredaM nAstItyAdirUpeNa pratIyate | natu tau vinA kevala ityanvayavyatirekAbhyAmekaj~nAnasambandhena vyApyavyApakabhAvopapAdanametadityavagantavyam.h | prAtargajAdyabhAvaj~nAnaM tvanyathopapAdayiShyAmaH | 
kimato yadyevamabhAvasya vyApakaM sa dharmipratiyogitvamAkAshAttAvadvayAvarta(rtya)te | yasmAdAkAsha ityevAvagamyate na tvatredaM nAstIti | iyamapi (cha) vastuto mUrtAbhAvagocharaiva pratItiH pralayAdivannaJN.hvarjitAbhilApasambandhAdatAdR^ishIva prakAshata iti chenna | nIlAdipratiterapi tathAtvaprasaN^gAt.h | anAnubhAvikatvasyobhayatrApi sAmyAt.h | tathAcha parasyApyasiddhayAdyApAtaH | vyApakanivR^ittyA(cha) vyApyanivR^ittiravashyaMbhAvinItyAkAshasya nAbhAvatvamiti | tadayaM prayogaH | AkAsho nAbhAvaH dharmipratiyoginau vinaiva pratIyamAnatvAdrUpavaditi | kiJNcha mUrtAbhAvamAkAshaM vadatA yo dharmI tasyochyate sa evAsmAkamAkAsha iti nAmnayeva vivAdo.avashiShyate | vakShyate chaitadviyadadhikaraNa iti |
sUtradvayArthamupasaMharati- svIkAreti ||
adR^iShyasya kShaNikatvAdeH svIkR^iti(kAra)to dR^iShyasya sthiratvAdestyAgataH | asau saugataH | adhikaM svata iti sheShaH | unmattamapi svasmAdadhikavivekavantaM (sthA)khyApayatItyarthaH | na hyunmattaH sarvatrApramitaM svIkaroti nApi pramitaM tyajatIti |
nanu (cha) yadi nIlAdikaM na syAttadA sanna syAt.h | arthakriyAkAritvaM hi sattvam.h | vyAptaM cha kramayaugapadyAbhyAm.h | tR^itIyaprakArAbhAvAt.h | nacha sthire tatsambhavaH prasaN^gatadviparyayAbhyAm.h | tathAhi | sthAyIbhAvaH kiM (svI)svakIyAmarthakriyAM krameNa kuryAdyugapadvA | Adye kAlAntarabhAvinImarthakriyAM pratIdAnIM samartho na vA | prathame tAmapIdAnIM(nImeva) kuryAt.h | samarthasya kShepAyogAt.h | dvitIye tadA.api na kuyarAt.h | idAnImasamartho.api tadAnIM samarthatvAtkariShyatIti chet.h | tadA sAmarthyAsAmarthyalakShaNaviruddhadharmAdhyAso bhAvaM bhindyAt.h | dvitIye tvAdyakShaNa eva kartavyasya sarvasya kR^itatvAt.h dvitIyAdikShaNe.asattvamavarjanIyameva | tadevamanukUlatarkabalalabdhapratibandhasya kShaNikatvAnumAnasya balavattvAtpratyabhij~nApratyanumAne tadbAdhite na sthairyasAdhanAyAlamiti |

tathAhi | yadyAtmAnAtmaprapaJNchaH sarvo.api kShaNikaH syAttadA pramA.apramArUpaH sarvo(kalo).apyanumAnAgamapratyabhij~nAlakShaNo vyavahAro lupyeta | tarkasyApyasya notthAnaM syAt.h | tasya tajjAtIyasya vA tena tajjAtIyena vA saha bhUyaH sambandhAvagame (na)ta tAdAtmyatadutpattyavadhAraNena (vA) chopAdhyabhAvA(dya)vadhAraNena vA vyabhichArAbhAvanishchaye sati vyAptyavadhAraNam.h | avadhR^itavyApteshcha pakShadarshanaM liN^gadarshanaM cha | tato.anubhUtavyAptismaraNam.h | atha yanmayA vyAptatvena j~nAtaM liN^gaM tadatra pakShe.astItyanusandhAnam.h | athedAnImanumitirityanumAnaprakriyA | na hyetatsarvaM kShaNikasyAtmanaH sambhavati | yena hi sakR^it.h dhUmo dR^iShyo naShya evAsau | kasya bhUyodarshanaM kasya cha vyAptyavadhAraNAdi | yasmiMshcha parvate dhUmo dR^iShyo naShya evAsau | kutra punarvyAptiliN^gAnusandhAnam.h | kutra cha sAdhyAdhyavasAyaH | 
evamAgame.apyekaikavarNashravaNAni, padAnusandhAnam.h, samayagrahaH, punaH padashravaNam.h, samayasmaraNam.h, vAkyArthaj~nAnamityanekasaMvi(kAnusandhA)ndhAnam.h, nAtmanaH kShaNikatAyAmupapadyate | pratyabhij~nAnamapi yena pUrvAvastho.artho 
j~nAtastenaiva tasya vA tatsadR^ishasya vA darshane bhavati | tatkathaM kShaNikasyAtmanaH syAt.h | anumAnena tarko.api vyAkhyAtaH | pratikShaNamAtmano.anAtmanashcha bhede.apyanumA(nA)dyaN^gIkAre.atiprasaN^gaH syAt.h | yasya kasyachidvayAptij~nAne nArikeladvIpavAsino.apyagnipramA (bhavet.h) syAt.h | parvate liN^gadarshanena hrade.apyagniranumIyetetyAdi | pUrvottarakShaNavartinAmAtmanAM parvatAdInAM cha kAryakAraNabhAvAdupapanno.anumAnAdivyavahAra iti chet.h(na) | anyatvasyAnapAyAt.h | anyathopAdhyAyashiShyabuddhayAdAvapi prasaN^gAt.h | 
atha matam.h | kAraNakShaNAH kAryakShaNeShu saMskArAnaparyanti | ataH pUrvapUrvAtmasaMskArayoginAmuttarottareShAmAtmanAmanumAnAdivyavahAro yujyate | parvatAdayo.api (pUrva)pUrvasaMskArabhAjaH pakShAditvamashnuvate iti | etannirAkaraNAya sUtram.h | OM uttarotpAde cha pUrvanirodhAt.h OM || iti | tadvayAchaShye- uttareti ||
kasyachit.h kAraNasya, kachit.h kArye | tataH kimityata Aha- ata iti ||
AtmanaH kShaNikatvAtsaMskArAparNasya chA(vA)sambhavAdityarthaH | yanmayA vyAptatvena j~nAtaM tadatra vidyata ityAdi yathA bhavati tathA na j~neyaM j~nAtumashakyam.h | tatashchAnumA kutaH | AgamAderapyupalakShaNametat.h | 
nanvasti tAvadanumAnAdivyavahAraH, sarvalokasiddhasyApahnavAyogAt.h | tadbalenAlaukikamapyasahabhAvinaH saMskArArpakatvaM kalpayiShyata ityata Aha- ekatvamiti ||
kimanumAnAdivyavahArAnyathA.anupapattimAtreNAlaukikaM kalpanIyam.h, kiMvA.a.atmAdeH kShaNikatve.api sati | nAdyaH | AtmAdeH sthAyitvenaiva tadupapatteH | dvitIyastu syAt.h | yadyAtmAdeH kShaNikatvaM siddhaM syAt.h | nacha tadasti | pramANabAdhitatvAnniShpramANakatvAchcheti bhAvaH | ekatvaM bhidetyatra pUrvottarakAlayoriti sheShaH | anubhUtisthaM pratyabhij~nAsiddham.h | kuto.aN^gIkAryetyadhyAhArAtsamAnakartR^itAsiddhiH | 
nanu cha pratyabhij~nAnaM bhrAntamityuktam.h | tatkathamAtmAderaikyaM tataH siddhayedityata Aha- valyeveti ||
tarkabalenAnumAne niravakAshatayA prabale sati hi tadvirodhAtpratyabhij~nAnaM bhrAntaM syAt.h | yadA tu tarkasyoktavidhayA.a.abhAsatvaM, tadA kutaH kShaNikatvAnumAnaprAbalyam.h | kutashcha pratyabhij~nAyAstadbAdhaH | abAdhitashcha pratyabhij~nAnubhavo yato balyeva | ata AtmAderekatvaM tena siddhamiti sambandhaH | etenAnumAnasiddhasya bhedasya kathaM nirmAnakatvamityapi parAstam.h | tadupajIvyasya tarkasyAdyApyanavasthAnAt.h | 
nanvastUttarotpAda eva pUrvasya nirodhastathA.api kutaH pUrvasyottarasminsaMskArAnAdhAyakatvamityata Aha- kAryakAraNayoshcheti ||
uttarotpAda eva pUrvasya nirodhAtkAyarkAraNayorekakAlInatvaM tAvannAstIti labhyate | ekakAlInatvaM cha vinA pUrvAhitasaMskArayogitvamuttarasya na yujyate | niyamena chetyanena kvachidapi na yujyate kutaH sarvatreti sUchayati | yadvaikakAlInasya eva saMskArArpakatvaM dR^iShyaM na bhinnakAlatva iti vyApterityarthaH | 
nanvekakAlInatvAbhAve.api kutaH saMskArArpakatvaM na syAdityata Aha- sambaddhA eveti ||
yasmAt.h akhilAH saMskArAdhAyakAshchAmpakakusumAdayaH padArthAstailAdibhiH sambaddhA eva anyatra tailAdau saMskAramAdadhate, nAsambaddhA ityasti niyamaH | nacha bhinnakAlIna(la)yoH sambandho yujyate | tasmAduttareNashasambaddhaH pUrvastasminnuttare vAsanAM na kuryAditi |
uktamarthaM buddhayArohArthaM saN^kalayyAha- ekakAlatayeti ||
atraikakAlatayA vinA kAryakAraNayoryogo na yujyate | yogaM vinA kAraNasya kArye saMskArArpakatvaM cha na ghaTate, saMskArato vinA kathamanumAnAdivyavahAra ityadhyAhAreNa yojanA | saMskArAparkatvaM cha na ghaTate, saMskArato vinA kathamanumAnAdivyavahAra ityadhyAhAreNa yojanA | yadIdaM saN^kalanaM na kriyeta tadA pUrvo(ktahetUnAM)ktAnAM pratyekaM saMskArAnAdhayakatve hetutvaM j~nAyeta | sarvatra sAdhyanirdeshAt.h tatra ko doShaH | uktAkAN^kShAkuNThitatvameveti |
atraite prayogAH | pUrvakShaNa uttarakShaNe saMskArAdhAyako na bhavati, tenAsambaddhatvAt.h | yo yenAsambaddho nAsau tatra saMskArAdhAyakaH, yathA sampratipannaH | yadvA yo yatra saMskArAdhAyakaH sa tatsambaddha eva dR^iShyo yathA sammataH | asambaddhasyApi saMskArAdhAyakatve mR^igamado vasanamiva sarvaM vAsayedavisheShAt.h | asambaddhashcha pUrva uttareNa | tato bhinnakAlInatvAt.h | sampratipannavat.h | bhinnakAlInayorapi sambandhe.atiprasaN^gaH | bhinnakAlInashcha pUrvaM uttareNa | tadutpAda eva vinaShyatvAt.h | saMmatavat.h | prAgeva naShyasya tenaikakAlInatvashaN^kA eva vyAhateti | nanu lAkShArasAhitabIjapUrakusumalauhityavatkinna syAditi 
chet.h(na) | tatrApi niranvayavinAshotpAdAnabhyupagamAt.h | atra cha parasiddhanyAyena parasya bodhanAnnAshrayAsiddhayAdi shaN^kanIyamiti |
bhavedetadyadi kAraNasya kAryotpAda eva vinAshaH syAt.h | sa eva kutaH siddha ityata Aha- kShaNamAtramiti ||
kAryakAraNayostAvaduttarapUrvatvamAvashyakam.h | yaugapadye kAyarkAraNabhAvavyAghAtAt.h | tataH pUrvakShaNavarti kAraNaM yadi kAyarkShaNe.api syAttadA sarvavastUnAmaN^gIkR^itaM kShaNamAtramavasthAnaM bhajyeta | ataH kShaNikatvAbhyupagama evottarotpAde cha pUrvanirodhaM gamayatIti |
syAdetat.h | kAraNaM kShaNasya pUrvavibhAge labdhasattAkaM madhyavibhAge kAryamutpAdyAparavibhAge tatra saMskAramAdhAya nashyatItyaN^gIkAre na ko.api doSha ityata Aha- pUrveti || 
atra vibhAgamAtraM kalochyate | pUrvAparayorabhAve tannirUpyamadhyAbhAvaH siddhaH | iShyate saugataiH | 
evaM tarkasya pratitarkaparAhatimabhidhAyedAnIM yathA sthAyinaH sattvAnupapattirevaM kShaNikasyApi tadanupapatteranukUlatA nAma tarkadoSha iti pratipAdayituM sUtram.h OM asati pratij~noparodho yaugapadyamanyathA OM || iti | tadvayAchakShANastAvadvikalpena tatpR^ichChati- pUrveti ||
arthakriyAkAritvaM hi sattvaM parasyAbhimatam.h | tachcha vakShyamANa(vi)kalpadvaya(yena)vyAptam.h | tR^itIyaprakArAnirUpaNAt.h | nacha tatkShaNike sambhavati | tathAhi kShaNikAdbhAvAdbhavatkAryaM kiM pUrvasya kAraNasya bhAve bhavati | kAraNasattAsamAnakAlInasattamiti yAvat.h | uta tasya kAraNasya nAshe sati sambhavatIti |
Adye doShamAha- yaugapadyamiti ||
sati kAraNe | kAryaM bhavati chet.h tarhIti sheShaH | kShaNikaM hi kAraNam.h | kAryaM cha tatsattAsamAnakAlInasattaM chetkAryakAraNayoH sahotpAda ityuktaM syAt.h | kShaNe vibhAgAbhAvasyoktatvAt.h tattatkAyarANAmapyayameva nyAya iti tatsantAnabhAvinA(pya)masheShakAyarANAM yaugapadyaM syAt.h | tachcha pratyakShAdiviruddhamiti | atra yadyapi yugapadbhavatoH kAryakAraNabhAvAnupapattirapi dUShaNam.h | tathA.api tachChiShyaireva j~nAtuM shakyata iti, "ubhayathA cha doShAt.h' iti sUtre kathitamiti vA(chA)tra noktam.h |
dvitIyaM nirAkaroti- vinAshe chediti ||
kAraNasya kAryaM bhavettarhIti sheShaH | tattasya kAryaM na bhavatItyApannam.h | anyathA sarvasya sarvaM kAyarM syAt.h | na hyAnantaryamAtreNa kAryakAraNabhAvaH | tathAtve vinAshakAryatvaprasaN^gAt.h | AnantaryasyAnyApekShayA.api sattvAt.h | sAdeshyAderapAkR^itatvAt.h | evamanyasyApi kAryaM na bhavatIti na kAryaM syAdakAraNaM vA | ubhayathA.api pUrvasyArthakriyAvirahAdasattvaprAptiriti | sUtrakR^itA saugatAbhyupagataM pakShaM pradhAnIkR^itya dUShaNamuktam.h | bhAShyakR^itA tvabhAvasya bhAvasApekShatvAttena krameNAto.arthavirodhAbhAvaH | 
nanvasti tAvatpratikShaNaM kAryotpattiH | nacha kAryaM kAraNena vinotpattumalam.h | tathA sati nityaM sattvamasattvaM ve(che)tyApatteH | ataH kAryotpattirevAnyatarapakShadoShamAbhAsayiShyati | pakShAntaraM vA grAhayiShyatItyata Aha- kAryotpattau cheti ||
syAdetadyadi pratikShaNaM kAryotpattiH pramANavatI syAt.h | na chaitadasti | nacha svAN^gIkAramAtreNArthAntarAkShepasAmarthyamatiprasaN^gAditi | nanvasti, yatsattatkShaNikaM yathA dehAdi, sachcha vivAdapadamiti pratikShaNaM kAryotpattau pramANamiti chenna | asyaiva nirAkriyamANatvAt.h | dehAdInAma(deha)pi kShaNikatvAbhAvena dR^iShyAntasya sAdhyavikalatvAchcha |
nanu dehAdeH pUrvottarakShaNayoH parimANabhedena bhedasiddhau kShaNikatvasiddhirityuktamityasya Aha- abhede.apIti || 
pUrvottarakShaNayoriti sheShaH | visheSheNa ArambhavAdadvailakShaNyena | AdipadenAN^kurAdi | visheShadarshanaM parimANabhedadarshanam.h | asmAkaM pariNAmavAdinAM mate | ayamatharH | ArambhavAdino hi parimANaM yAvaddravyabhAvyabhyupayanti | avayavasaN^khayAtishayAnatishayAyattatvAtparimANabhedasya | avayavApachaye dravyavinAshasyAvayavopachaye cha tadutpAdasyAvarjanIyatvAt.h | atasteShAM parimANabhedo dravyaM bhindyAdeva | asmAkaM tvavasthitameva dravyamavayavopachayApachayAbhyAM ta(tta)tparimANakatayA vikriyata iti darshanam.h | tatra parimANabhedo na bhedamAkShipatIti | 
kiJNcha phalAdInAM pUrvottarakShaNayorbhedaH sAdhyate, utAbhedAbhAvaH | Adye siddhasAdhanam.h | bhedasyAsmAbhirapyaN^gIkR^itatvAt.h | tAvatA kShaNabhaN^gAsiddheH | dvitIye doShamAha- anubhUtita iti ||
tadidaM phalamiti pratyabhij~nayA pUrvottarakShaNayorabhedasiddherbAdhitaviShayamanumAnamiti sheShaH | bhrAntA pratyabhij~nA nAbhedaM sAdhayitumalamiti chet.h | tarhi bhrAntaM parimANabhedadarshanaM na bhedasAdhanAyAlamiti brUmaH | parimANabhedadarshanaM bAdhakAbhAvAtpramANameveti chettatrAha- visheSheti ||
tarhi sthairyadR^ikkuto na mAnam.h | tasyA api bAdhakarahitatvAt.h | visheShadarshanaM bAdhakamiti chet.h | tarhi sthairyadarshanaM kuto na bAdhakam.h | ato.anupalabhyamAnavisheShayo(ranayo)rbAdhyabAdhakabhAvAyogAdanyonyapratipakShatAnanubhavAchchAnyatarapakShapAtaM parityajya bhedAbhedaviShayatayaiva vyavasthApanaM yuktam.h | anyathA dR^iShyAnte sAdhyasandehenApi parAnumAnaM duShyaM syAditi | evaM tarkAN^gAntaravaikalyaM svayamUhanIyam.h |
nanvetAni sUtrANi kuto vyutkrameNa(mato)vyAkhyAtAni | uchyate | upodghAtaprakriyayA sUtrakAreNaivAdau bAdhakAni nirAkR^ityAnte niShkaNTakA pratyabhij~nopanyastA | bhAShyakAreNa tu subodhatvAya shiShyAkAN^kShAkrameNAdau pratyabhij~nAmabhidhAyAnantaraM tadbAdhakAni parihR^itAnIti |
duHkhAbhAvaM sukhaM chAhuriti yadanUditaM tannirAkaroti- digiti ||
svadR^iShyAntAdityAkAshasya bhAvatve yo nyAyo.abhihitastasmAditi hetvatideshaH | dharmipratiyoginirapekShameva vidhirUpeNa pratIyamAnatvAdityarthaH | sadbhAvaH kvachidbhavechchettaddR^iShyAnteneti sheShaH | anenAnyathA rUpAdinAmapi bhAvatvaM na syAdavisheShAditi bAdhakaM sUchayati | yadyapi disho nAkAshAdbhidyante | tathA.apyAkAshasya bhAgasadbhAvaM j~nApayituM tAsAM grahaNam.h | ekavachanaM tu jAtyabhiprAyam.h | 
etenAkAshe chAvisheShAditi sUtraM prakArAntareNa vyAkhyAtaM bhavati | AkAshAdInAM bhAvatvasamarthanena paJNchaskandhAtmakaM vishvamiti nirastam.h | Atmano j~nAnAtmakatvaM tu nAsmAkaM aniShyam.h(viruddham.h) | kShaNabhaN^gitAyA nirastatvAt.h | j~nAnasyApi grAhakatAyAH pareNAbhyupagatatvAt.h | mokShastu chaturthe parIkShiShyate | 
syAdetat.h | vaibhAShikasautrAntikayoryaH sAdhAraNaH svamataviruddhaH siddhAntaH sa eva nirAkR^itaH | yastu sautrAntikasya siddhAntavisheShaH "pramANaM tAvadvividham.h | prameyadvaividhyAt.h | tatra j~nAnAtiriktaH sarve.api rUpAdiprapaJNcho.anumeya eva na tu pratyakShaH | j~nAnaM (tu) nIlAdyAkAraM pratyakShavedyam.h' iti | sa kasmAnna nirAkR^ita ityata Aha- vishvamiti ||
tayoH vaibhAShikasautrAntikayormadhye yaH sautrAntiko vishvaM rUpAdikaM pratyakShagaM tyaktvA rUpAdervishvasya pratyakShavedyatAM vaibhAShikAdibhirabhyupagatAmanabhyupagamyeti yAvat.h | anumitaM vadet.h rUpAdervishvasyAnumAnavedyatAmaN^gIkuryAt.h | mAyAvAdinA tulyaM vartata iti mAyAvAdivat.h | etaduktaM bhavati | yathA sarvAnduHsamayAnapAkurvatA(.api) sUtrakR^itA na mAyAvAdo.atra pAde nirAkR^itaH | tasyAtyantanirdalasyopekShaiva kAryA | na tvIShatsadalaiH sAN^khayAdisamayaiH saha nirAsa iti j~nApanArtham.h | tathA bAhyAnumeyatAvAdo.apIti | nanu mAyAvAdaH sUtrotpattyuttarakAlabhAvI | tasya kathaM nirAsaprasaktiH | maivam.h | "anAdikAlato vR^ittAH' ityaktatvAt.h | anyathA sAN^khayAdinirAsasyApyaprasakteriti | JOSHI-3
nanvapratiShiddhamanumAnaM bhavatIti nyAyena nIlAdervishvasyApratyakShatvaM sUtrakArasyAbhimatameveti kuto na kalpyate | (naivaM) nachaivaM shakyam.h | pramANAviruddhaH pramANAnusArI cha sUtrakArasyAbhiprAyaH kalpanIyaH | nachAyamarthastathetyAshavAnAha- sarveti ||
ayamatrottarakramaH | nIlAderarthasyApratyakShatvaM na vaktuM shakyate | nIlAdipratIteraparokShatAyAH sAkShisiddhatvAt.h | indriyavyApArabhAvabhAvitvenAnumAnasiddhatvAchcha | atha matam.h | yenArthena yajj~nAnaM jAyate tat.h tadAkAraM bhavati | tachcha j~nAnaM svaprakAshatayA svagataM nIlAdyAkAramapi sAkShAtkurute | ato.aparokShatayopalabhyamAnasya nIlAdyAkAranikarasya buddhigatatvAnna kashchiddoSha iti | atredamupatiShThate | yadaparokShatayA.avabhAsamAnaM nIlAdyAkArachakraM buddherbhedena sarvadA sarvapramANasiddham.h | tasya kathaM nu buddhitvamaN^gIkriyate | bahirmukhatayedantena hyayaM nIlAdyAkAro.aparokShamavabhAsate | na jAtvantarmukhatayA.ahaM nIlamiti | tathA nIlAparokShaj~nAnasamanantaraM nIlArthI niyamena bahiH pravartate | tenAnumIyate.anena bahirartha eva sAkShAtkR^ita iti | na hyanyatra j~nAnamanyatra pravR^ittiriti yujyate | atiprasaN^gAt.h | madhye.anumAnaM tu nirasiShyate | evamApto.api kimaparokShatayA pashyasIti pR^iShyo.aN^guliM prasAryedamiti bAhyameva bravItyatastribhirapi pramANairaparokShatayA.avabhAsamAnasya nIlAdyAkArasya buddhito bheda evAvasIyate | na chedaM sarvaM bhrAntam.h | kadA.apyanyathApratItyabhAvAt.h | vinaiva bAdhakena bhrAntitvAbhyupagame.atiprasaN^gAt.h | ato.aparokShatayA.avabhAsamAno nIlAdyAkAro bAhya eva, natu buddhigata iti |
kiJNcha bAhyArthasyApratyakShatve tadasiddhireva syAt.h | pramANAbhAvAt.h | tathAcha bAhyArthAbhyupagamo riktaH syAdityAha- vishvamiti 
||
anyat.h j~nAnamiti sheShaH | kA pramA yasya tat.h kiMpramam.h | anumeyo bAhyAkAra iti chet.h(na) | sarvathA.asiddhasya pakShIkaraNAyogAt.h | liN^gAbhAvAdvayAptyasiddheshcha | syAdetat.h | buddhigatastAvadAkAro.aparokShamavabhAsate | sa kAdAchitkatvAtkimapi kAraNamepakShamANo bAhyaM nIlAdyanumApayiShyatIti | maivam.h | bAhyatayaiva nIlAdyAkArasya sphuraNAt.h | kutra chedamulabdham.h, yatkAdAchitkaM tatkAraNavaditi | j~nAna eveti chet.h(na) | bAhyApratyakShatvavAde tatrApi kAraNatvAnavadhAraNAt.h | j~nAnaM pUrvaj~nAnakAraNakamupalabdhamiti chet.h | tarhyAkAro.api pUrvAkArajanyaH kalpyatAm.h | kiM bAhyArthavyasanena | nIlaj~nAnAnaM(notpAdAna)ntaraM pItaj~nAnotpAdadarshanAnneti chet.h(na) | sadR^ishajanyatvasya pareNa kvApyanupa(gantavya)labdhatvAt.h |
kiJNcha vAsanAdikamAntarameva sahakArIkR^itya visadR^isha(meva)mapi j~nAnaM janayatIti kalpanIyam.h | na bAhyam.h | dR^iShyenaiva kathaJNchidupapattAvadR^iShyakalpanAnupapatteH | ato bAhyo.a(pya)rthaH pratyakShasiddha iti shaN^kAnAspadatvAdidaM matamatra na dUShitamityuktam.h | yadvA sphuTatarAnalpadoShatvena shiShyaireva heyatayA j~nAtuM shakyatvAdityAshayenAha- sarveti ||

nanu kimarthamayaM paramatopanyAsaH | bhedapArthakyamantareNa visheShapratItAvasmAkama(pyevame)pyayameva parihAra iti j~nApanArtham.h | tarhIdameva vAkyaM tathA vyAkhyAyatAm.h | nai(chai)vaM (shaM)shakyam.h | tadbhedashcheti pR^ithagbhedagrahaNavirodhAt.h | visheShaNavisheShyabhAvena grahaNamapi na dharmipratiyogiprakArAdbhidyata iti vaisheShikaparIkShAyAmuktam.h | ato nAtra vyutpAdanamapi kR^itamiti |

anyachchetyarthaH | kathamiti chet.h | kimatra yadi dharmyAdipratItyapekShayA bhedaH pratIyeta tadA.anyonyAshrayatvaM syAdi(tyA)tyevApAdyate, kiMvA yadi bhedaH pratIyeta tadA.anyonyAshrayatvaM syAditi | 
Adye doShamAha- bheda iti ||
kathamityAkShepe | paripR^ichChatIti mR^idUktiH | AkShipatIti yAvat.h | dharmyAdibhedagrahaNAt.h dharmyAdigrahaNasApekShabhedagrahaNAt.h | kathamidaM labhyate | dharmyAdipadasya tadgrahaNopalakShaNatvAt.h | Adipadasya cha kAraNArthasyA.a.avR^itteH | tadetatparasparaM vyAhatamiti sheShaH | tathAhi | bhedo durgraha iti pratij~nAya tadupapattaye hIdamuchyate | anena cha yadi bhedo dharmyAdipratItimapekShya pratIyeta tadA.anyonyAshrayatvaM syAt.h | tathAcha na pratIyetetyApAdanena pratIyate chAto na dharmyAdigrahaNApekShA tatpratItiriti labdhaM bhavet.h | tathAcha "bhedo durgrahaH'"pratIyate cha' ityetayoH kathaM na pUrvottaravirodha iti |
dvitIye pR^ichChAmaH | kiM pareNa kvApi bhedo na gR^ihItaH kiMvA kvachid.hgR^ihIta iti | AdyaM dUShayati- anyatveti ||
yadyanyatvaM kvApi na gR^ihItaM tadA.anyonyAshrayatvApAdanameva na shakyam.h | nirAshrayatvAt.h | taddhi pratItayordvayoH kAryakAraNabhAvAshrayaNe satyApadyate | antato vAdiprativAdinoH dUShyadUShakayorApAdyApAdakayorbhedAgrahe.anutthAnamevApAdanasya | dvitIyaM dUShayati- anyatvamiti ||
siddhaM pratItam.h | anyonyAshrayatve hi bhedapratItireva na syAt.h | nahyanyonyAshrayANi kAryANi kvApi dR^iShyAni prakalpyante | tathAchAsti chedbhedapratItiH nUnamAbhAsabhUtamevedamanyonyAshrayatvamapratibandhakatvAditi | asti bhedapratItiH sA na prameti tu tAtparyamiti chenna kimanyonyAshrayatvamanyonyotpAdaM pratibadhanAtIti mataM, kiMvA taddharmam.h | Adye kathamapramA.api bhedapratItirutpadyate | na dvitIyaH | anyayoranyonyAshrayatvamanyattu lupyata ityasyAnyAyatvAt.h | sAMvR^itI pra(tIti)tipattiriti chet.h | tatkiM paTa; sAMvR^ita iti yebhyastantubhyo jAtasteShAmeva kAraNaM bha(va)viShyatIti |
nanvanenAsya tarkasya kiM dUShaNamuktaM syAdityata Aha- etAdR^ishasyeti ||
na kevalametajjAtyuttaraM kintu yadanyadapi tadIyaM vachanam.h | tathAhi | bhedasyApi bhedAntarabhedyatve.anavastheti | tathA bhinne bhedaniveshashchettenaiva bhedena bhinnatAyAmAtmAshrayatvaM, bhedAntarAN^gIkAre tvanavasthA | abhinne bhedaniveshashchetsvato.api paTasya bhedApattiriti |
tathA na tAvatpratyakSheNa bheda eva dR^ishyate | bheda ityeva pratIteranubhavAt.h | vastuno.api pratItau na tAvadbhedapUrvaM vastupratItiH | uktadoShAt.h | nApi vastupratItipUrvikA bhedapratItiH | abhedena pratIte bhedapratItAvatiprasakteH | nacha yugapat.h | bhedapratItiM prati vastupratIteH kAraNatvena yaugapadyAyogAt.h | nacha prakArAntaramastIti |
tathA sattAvatkAraNaM vA kAraNe sattA vA | Adye kAraNasyAsattvam.h | dvitIye.asata eva kAraNatvamityAdi | 
tatsarvaM jAtyuttaramiti j~nApayitumetAdR^ishasyetyuktam.h | sarvasyApi svavyAghAtakatvAt.h | bhedasya sattAyAshcha svarUpAtiriktayorayuktayoH (ktAyAH) (ktatAyAH) ayuktAyAH) evAN^gIkaraNAchcha | 
katameyaM jAtiriti chenna | sAmAnyalakShaNasadbhAve.asya nirbandhasya vyarthatvAt.h | ahetuprasaN^ganityasamAsvantarbhAvAchcha |
mAyAshabdasya vrIhyAditvAnmAyIti sAdhuH | shUnyavAdinirAse(naiva)na mAyAvAdo.api nirasto veditavya ityatideshaj~nApanAya mAyI chetyuktam.h | evashabdasyottaratrata sambandhaH | 
nanvetadanyonyAshrayatvAdikaM sUtrakR^itaiva kuto na nirAkR^itamityata Aha- taditi ||
tasmAjjAtyuttarAkaratvAdupekShyAveva | natu parihArAya prativAdIkartavyau | etaduktaM bhavati | sadalameva pUrvapakShivachanaM nirAkartavyaM bhavati na nirdalam.h | anyathA.atiprasaN^gAt.h | etachcha jAtyuttaratvena nirdalamityupekShitaM sUtrakR^itA | asmAbhistu shiShyavyutpAdanAya nirAkR^itamiti |
syAdetat.h | shUnyAvAdI shUnyaM jagatkAraNaM manyate | mAyAvAdI tu brahma | tatkathaM nAsato.adR^iShyatvAdityAdishUnyavAdanirAsAya mAyAvAde.atideshaH | matavaiShamye.atideshAsambhavAdityata Aha- yadIti || 
tasmAdatidesho yukta iti sheShaH | tatkathamityata Aha- nahIti ||
lakShaNabhedena hi vipratipanno bhedo bodhanIyaH | nA(chA)sau shUnyabrahmaNoH sambhavati | dvayorapi nirvisheShatvAN^gIkArAt.h | 
nanu nirvisheShatvena bAhyalakShaNabhedAbhAve.api satyaj~nAnAnantAnandAtmakatvaM brahmaNaH svalakShaNaM mAyAvAdinA.aN^gIkR^itam.h | na shUnyasya shUnyavAdinA | tena brahmashUnyayorbhedo bhaviShyatItyata Aha- anR^itAdIti ||
brahmaNaH satyaj~nAnAdyAtmakatvaM nAmAnR^itajaDAdivirodhitvamevAbhimataM mAyAvAdino.anyasyAsambhavAt.h, "anR^itajaDavirodhirUpamantatrayamalabandhanaduHkhatAviruddham.h' iti tad.h vyAkhyAnAchcha | anR^itAdivirodhitvaM cha shUnyavAdI shUnyasyApi manyate | "jADyasaMvR^itiduHkhAntapUvardoShavirodhi yat.h' iti vachanAt.h | tato naitadapi bhedakamiti yukta evAtideshaH | 
syAdetat.h | prapaJNchamithyAtvAnumAnanirAsArthaM vaidharmyAchcha na svapnAdivaditi sUtram.h | tatra yat.h "bhrAnteH saMvR^ivisatyasya' iti dUShaNamuktam.h | tadeva vaidharmyAditi sUtre pratIyate | yatpunaruktaM dR^ishyatvasya satyatve tatraiva vyabhichAraprasaN^gAttasya mithyAtvaM vAchyam.h | tathAchAsAdhakatvamiti tatsUtre na dR^ishyate | tatkathametadvayAkhyAnamityata Aha- svavAkyeti ||
atra vAkyamiti hetuvAkyArtho dR^ishyatvaM lakShyate | tatpakSha iti viShayasaptamI | tanmithyAtvasAdhanaviShaya iti yAvat.h | iti shabdo hetau | aprayatnAt.h prayatnamavidhAya, "vaidharmyAchcha na svapnAdivat.h' ityanena nirAchakra iti sambandhaH | etaduktaM bhavati | dR^ishyatvasya mithyAtvaM shUnyavAdinaivAbhyupagatam.h | mithyAbhUtasyA(chA)sAdhakatvaM suprasiddhameva | ata e(vai)tadviShaye sadvAdinaH kimapi kR^ityaM nAstyeva | sphuTadUNavyutpAdane sUtratvavyAghAtAt.h | tasmAdetaddUShaNavyutpAdane sUtrakR^itA prayatno na vihitaH | asmAbhistu tadabhiprAyaH sphuTIkR^ita iti |
tathA.api "sattvaM chAsyAnubhUShitaH' iti yatprapaJNchamithyAtvasya pratyakShaviruddhatvamuktam.h | yachcha "mithyAtve mA na kAchana' iti niShpramANatvaM, tadubhayaM sUtre na dR^ishyata ityata Aha- cheti ||
asya mithyAtvasya | nanvanuktasamuchchayArthena chashabdenedaM dUShaNadvayaM sUchitamiti yathA vyAkhyAyate | tathA tadapi chAshabdArthatayA vyAkhyAyatAm.h | kimanuktatvAN^gIkAreNa | maivam.h | "na kR^ityaM prativAdinaH' ityuktvAt.h | sUtre hetuvisheShasyAnupAdAnAnniShpramANakatvaM j~nApitamityastu | kiM chAshabdasyobhayasUchakatvagrahaNena | na | sati shabde sAvakAshaj~nApakAdaraNAnupapatteH | svapnAdivaditi sUtraM svapnavaditi vyAkhyAtam.h | ko.atrAbhiprAyaH | uchyate | bahusthaleShu gR^ihIteyaM vyAptirityato na vyabhichAramarhatIti pUrvapakShiNo.abhimAnaM sUchayituM sUtrakAreNAdipadaM prayuktam.h | tathA.api prayogavelAyAmeka eva dR^iShyAnta upAdeyo.anyathA.a.adhikyaM prasa(jyate)jyeteti | yathA.a.aha | hetUdAharaNAdikam.h adhikamiti | etajj~nApanAya bhAShyakAreNa svapnavadityevoktamiti sarvaM sustham.h | 
|| iti shrImannyAyasudhAyAM asadadhikaraNam.h ||
|| atha shrImannyAyasudhAyAM anupalabdhyadhikaraNam.h ||
|| OM na bhAvo.anupalabdheH OM || atra yogAchArANAM matamapAkriyate | tadarthaM tadupanyasyati- j~nAnameveti ||
vij~nAnameva tattvaM, na rUpAdayashchatvAraH skandhAH, iti yogAchArA manyanta ityatharH | vij~nAnAN^gIkAre.api visheShamAha- ekamiti || advitIyamityarthaH | nanu j~neyamapi rUpAdikaM pratyakShAdisiddhaM tatkathaM vij~nAnameva tattvamityata Aha- akhileti || j~nAnameva j~neyakAram.h | na j~neyaM nAma j~nAnAdbhinnamastItyarthaH | kuto j~neyasya j~nAnAtmakatvamityata Aha- prabhAsata iti || j~nAnaM hi prakAshate | tena prakAshamAnatvasya j~nAnatvena vyAptau siddhAyAM nIlAderapi prakAshamAnasya j~nAnatvaM siddhamityarthaH | yadvA 
prabhAsate nIlAdinA sahaiveti sheShaH | tena "sahopalambhaniyamAdabhedo nIlataddhiyoH' ityuktaM bhavati |
nanvayukto j~nAnaj~neyayorabhedaH | bhedasya pratibhAsanAt.h | ekamiti chAyuktam.h | vij~nAnasantatInAM bhedasya ekaikasyApi santatau vij~nAnabhedasya cha vidyamAnatvAt.h | kiJNcha AstAmanyo bhedaH | bhedAbhAvastAvadabhyupagamyate | tenaiva vij~nAnasya sadvitIyatvAprApternaikatvamupapadyata ityata Aha- tatreti ||
tatra j~nAnaj~neyayoH bheda iti sambandhaH | santatibhedaH santatInAM parasparaM bhedaH | svabhedaH ekaikasyAmapi santatau pUrvottaraj~nAnabhedaH | kalpitA eveti sambandhaH | nAnAsaMvR^itibhUmiShu anekAj~nAnasthAneShvantaHkaraNeShu | yadvA nAnAsaMvR^itikAraNakAsu vAsanAsviti nimittasaptamI | taduktam.h "bhedastu bhrantibuddhayaiva dR^i(dR^ishya indA)shyetendAvivAdvayaH' iti | 
evamanUditaM matamapAkaroti- ityetadapIti |
pUrvamatasamuchchayArtho.apishabdaH | 
anena "na bhAve' iti sUtrAMsho vyAkhyAtaH | jagat.h bhAvo j~nAnaM na bhavatItyarthaH | bhavateranubhavArthatvAt.h | upasargA hi dhAtulInAsyArthasya vyaJNjakA eva | 
kuto na yuktamiti chet.h | kiM j~neyaM svarUpeNAsadeva vij~nAne samAropitaM vij~nAnAtmaka(mityu)muchyate, kiM vA paramArthasata eva j~neyasya jagato vij~nAnAtmakatvaM bhedamAtraM tvasaditi | AdyastvatItAdhikaraNarItyA nirastaH | na dvitIyaH | jagato j~nAnAbhede pramANAbhAvAt.h | na tAvattatra pratyakShamastItyAha- na hIti ||
anenAnupalabdherityetadvayAkhyAtaM bhavati | mA bhUtpratyakSheNa j~nAnArthayorabhedasiddhiH | prakAshamAnatvAdyanumA(nAttu)nena tu bhaviShyatItyata Aha- anubhavasyaiveti ||
sambandhamAtre ShaShThI | evashabdenAnubhavasyAnumAnataH prAbalyaM sUchayati | tanmataM tadabhimatamanumAnamiti sheShaH | j~nAnaj~neyayoraikyamiti (cha) vA | j~nAnaj~neyayoH sphuTaM bhedasyaiva sAkShisiddhatvAtkAlAtyayApadiShyatvamanumAnasyetyarthaH | anenAnupalabdherityetadupalabdhivirodhAditi cha vyAkhyAtam.h |
nanu bhedagrAhakaM pratyakShaM bhrAntamiti chenna | bAdhakAbhAvAt.h | anumAnaM bAdhakamiti tu na vAchyam.h | pratyakShasyAnumAnato balavattvAt.h | anyathA kAlAtItatochChedaprasaN^gAt.h | pratyakShasya bhrA(nti)ntatve.anumAnaprAmANyaM tasmiMshcha pratyakShasya bhrAntatvamityanyonyAshrayatvAchcheti | 
anumAnavirodhaM chAnumAnasya pratipAdayituM sUtram.h OM kShaNikatvAchcha OM || iti | tadvayAchaShye- kShaNikatvAchcheti ||
AshutaravinAshitvAdityarthaH | nacha j~nAnasya kShaNikatvaM bhrAntam.h | abAdhitapra(tIti)tyayasiddhatvAt.h | sthirarUpataH AshutaravinAshitArahita(tvAt.h)tvataH | anusmR^iteshchetyAdyuktaprakAreNa | atra kShaNikatvAkShaNikatvalakShaNaviruddhadharmAdhyAsaM bhedahetuM vadatA.a.antarabAhyatvAdiraneko viruddhadharmasaMsarga upalakShito boddhavyaH | 
evaM pratyekaM nirAkR^itAni bauddhamatAni sAdhAraNadoSheNa dUShayituM sUtram.h- OM savarthA.anupapatteshcha OM || iti | tadvayAkhyAti- sarveti || 
shrutiprAmANyasya samarthitatvAdavaidikaM pratyapi shrutivirodhakathanaM yuktameva | abhyupagatashrutiprAmANyaM (shiShyaM) prati vA | teShAM pakShANAmashivatvamanena j~nApyata iti | nanvanubhUtivirodhaH prAgukta eva punaH kasmAduchyate | upasaMhArArthamityadoShaH | yadvA tadIyaprameyAntare.apIti | 
|| iti shrImannyAyasudhAyAM anupalabdhyadhikaraNam.h ||
|| atha shrImannyAyasudhAyAM naikasminnadhikaraNam.h || 
|| OM naikasminnasambhavAt.h OM || jainamatamatra nirAkriyate | nirAkAryAMshaj~nApanAya tadupanyasyati- Aheti ||
dvividhaM tAvadvishvaM, jIvAjIvAtmakaM nirIshvaram.h | tatpunaH ShaD.hdravyAtmakam.h | tAni cha dravyANi jIvadharmAdhamarpudgalakAlAkAshanAmAni | tatra jIvAstrividhAH | baddhA yogasiddhA muktAshcheti | dharmo gatiheturjagadvayApI | adharmaH sthitiheturvyApaka eva | pudgalo rUparasagandhasparshavat.h dravyam.h | tat.h dvividham.h | paramANurUpaM saN^ghAtarUpaM cha | kAlaH, abhUdbhavati bhaviShyatIti vyavahAraheturapyaNurUpaH | AkAsha eko.anantapradeshashcha | sa dvividho lokAkAsho.alokAkAshashcheti | (e)teShvaNuvyatiriktAnyastikAyashabdAni | anekadeshavartini dravye.astikAyashabda(pra)vR^itteH | te cha jIvAstikAyo dharmAstikAyo.adhamarAstikAyaH pudgalAstikAya AkAshAstikAya iti paJNcha | 
atra cha mokShopayoginaH sapta padArthA jIvAjIvAsravabandhanirjarasaMvaramokShAH | jIvo j~nAnadarshanasukhavIryaguNaH | ajIvo jIvopabhogyaM vastujAtam.h | asravaH tadbhogopakaraNamindriyAdikam.h | bandho dvividhaH | ghAtikAghAtikachatuShyayabhedAt.h | AdyaM jIvaguNAnAM j~nAnA(nandA)dInAM pratibandhakam.h | dvitIyaM sharIrasaMsthAnatadabhimAnatatsthititatprayuktasukhaduHkhahetubhUtam.h | nirjaro mokShasAdhanaM tapaH | saMvara indriya(nirodhaH) nigrahaH | mokShaH svAbhAvikAtmasvarUpAvirbhAvaH | mokShagrahaNenaiva mokShamArgo.api saN^gR^ihItaH | sa cha samyagj~nAnasamyagdarshanasamyakchArityAkh.hyaratnatrayAtmakaH | 
tadetadvishvaM saptabhaN^gi pratyekaM saptaprakArakamA(mityA)ha kShapaNakaH | katham.h | sadityekaprakAraH | asaditi dvitIyaH | dvayaM sadasadAtmakamiti tR^itIyaH | advayam.h avaktavyamiti chaturthaH | dvayAdvayamiti paJNchamaShaShThau | tatra sadavaktavyaM cheti paJNchamaH, asadavaktavyaM cheti ShaShThaH | atatsarvamiti saptamaH | sarvamiti sadasadAtmakam.h, ataditi avaktavyam.h | 
atra saptabhaN^gitvanirAsArthaM naikasminnasambhavAditi sUtraM vyAchaShye- naitaditi ||
etatsaptaprakAratvaM kutaH | asambhavAt.h | so.api kathaM, dR^iShyivirodhataH | sarvaM hi svopAdhau sat.h paropAdhAvasat.h | svarUpeNa bhAvo.anyAtmatvAdinA.abhAvaH | dravyarUpeNa nityamavasthAbhedena anityam.h | svarUpAdinA.abhinnaM svaguNAdinA bhinnAbhinnamityeva pratIyate | nAto.anyena prakAreNa | ato vyavasthayA niyamagrAhakapratyakShAdivirodhenAsambhavAdayuktamevAnekAntamatamiti |
nanvekAntadarshanasya mithyAdR^iShyitvena na tadvirodho.asambhavamAhavatItyata Aha- bhAveti ||
yena rUpeNetyasyaiva vivaraNaM bhAvAbhAvatayeti | tachcha vyavasthitasadasattvAdyupalakShaNaM boddhavyam.h | yadvA bhAvAbhAvatayA.anyena cha yena sattvAdi(nA)rUpeNeti yojanA | athavA yena bhAvAbhAvatayA rUpeNeti sAmAnAdhikaraNyena yojyam.h | yadi vA bhAvAbhAvatayetyasya visheShaNametat.h | yena vyavasthitena rUpeNeti | kena pramANenetyAkShepaH | bhavedetanniyamadarshanasya mithyAdR^iShyitvam.h | yadi dR^iShyasya niyamasya nivArakamanekAntasAdhakaM prabalapramANaM syAt.h | na chaitadasti | nacha bAdhakena vinA pratyayAnAM mithyAtvaM kalpayituM yuktamatiprasaN^gAditi |
niyamasya bAdhakamAshaN^kate- tattaditi ||
sadvAdino hi sattvaM vishvasya pramANaiH prAtiShThipastadanaN^gIkAre doShAMshcha nyarUpayan.h | evamasadvAdino.apyasattvasthApanaM tadanaN^gIkAre dUShaNaM cha vyutpAditavantaH | tathA.anye.api svapakShasAdhanaM tadanabhyupagame bAdhanaM cha kR^itavantaH | tathAcha yadi sa(tya)tvaM nAN^gIkriyate tadA tu tadupanyastaM pramANamuparudhyeta dUShaNaM chAnuShajyeta | evamasattvAdyanaN^gIkAre.api | atastaddoShaparihArArthaM tattatpramANAnusaraNArthaM cha tattadAtmatA vishvasya mayA svIkR^itA | tathAchAnekAnte prabalapramANasadbhAvAtkathaM niyame bAdhakAbhAva iti | pariharati- tairiti ||
tarhIti sheShaH | 
idamatra vaktavyam.h | sadvAdimatAnusaraNasamaye.asattvAdibhaN^gIraN^gIkaroShi (vA) na veti | evamasadvAdicharaNasharaNapraveshavelAyAM sattvAdiprakArAnUrIkaroShi vA na veti | evamanyeShvapi pakSheShu vikalpaH | yadyAdyastadA.asau achaladarshanaH sadA sakalapakShAN^gIkAravAn.h tairdoShairakhilai(tairakhilairdoShai)rlipyate | tathAhi | sadvAdino hi na kevalaM sattve pramANaM tadanaN^gIkAre cha dUShaNaM cha vyutpAdya nivR^ittAH | kintvasattvAdipakSheShu doShAnapi vyutpAditavantaH | evamasadvAdino.api nAsattve pramANaM tadanabhyupagame bAdhakaM chAbhidhAyaivoparatA, kinnAma sattvAdipakSheShu doShAnapi upapAditavantaH | evamanye.api | tathAcha sakalapakShakakShIkAre (tu) tattadvAdyuktapakShAntaradoShalepaH kathaM na syAt.h | atha manyase | na te doShAH kintvAbhAsAH | te cha nAnekAntavAdaM bAdhanta iti | tadA kathaM tAni pramANAni | anaN^gIkAre doShAshcha nAbhAsAH | (ye nAnuma)yenAnusaraNIyAH | tasamttattadvAdivyutpAditapramANAdyanusAreNa saptabhaN^gIraN^gIkurvANena taduktavipakShadoShAnusAreNa tatparityAgo.api kAryaH syAt.h | tathA chAN^gIkAraparityAgAbhyAmubhayata AkR^iShyo.ayaM kaShyAM dashAmAviShyaH syAt.h | nanvekAnto dvedhA | kramAkramabhedAt.h | tatra kramAnekAnte tAvannAN^gIkAraparityAgau viruddhau | akramAnekAnte.api yena rUpeNa nityatvaM tenaivAnityatvamityAdyanaN^gIkArAnna virodhaH | tathAcha saptabhaN^gayaN^gIkAriNA mayA tAni pramANAni dUShaNAni cha vyavasthApitAni bhavantIti noktadoShaH | maivam.h | tattatpramANAdInAM vyavasthAnarhatvAt.h | na khalu tatta(tpramANavA)dvAdibhistAni tAni pramANAdIni sAvakAshAnyupanyastAni | tasmAtsarveShvapi (vAdiShu) vAdeShu paramAstikasya kathitaiva gatiH | api chaivamapi saptabhaN^gayaN^gIkAro nirmUla eva | na hyevaMvAdino vAdinaH prasiddhAH | sambhAvanayA tadaN^gIkAre cha na saptatvapariniShThA | sambhAvanAvakA(ko)shasya niHsImatvAt.h | kiJNcha sarvAN^gIkArapakShe syAdasti cha nAsti cheti pakShAtsyAdasti syAnnAstIti pakShadvayaM na bhidyate |

etvantareNa shivasya vishvakartR^itvaM nirAkurvat.h OM adhiShThAnAnupapatteshcha OM || iti sUtraM vyAchaShye- adhiShThAna iti ||
yaH katarA kulAlAdiH sa pR^ithivyAdAvadhiShThAne sthita eva ghaTAdikAryaM kurvanpratIyate | natu niradhiShThAnaH kashchitkiJNchitkurvANaH | anena vyatirekAvinAbhAvena niradhiShThAnatvasyAkartR^itvena vyAptirupapAditA bhavati | tataH kimityata Aha- nAsyeti ||
asya shivasya | tadA AdisR^iShyisamaye | kuto nAsti | prAgutpannAnAM pR^ithivyAdInAM mahAbhUtAnAM pralaye sati | tasmAtkartR^itvamapi tasya nopapadyata iti sheShaH | nanu kArakANAmeva adhiShThAnatvaM bhaviShyati | maivam.h | sAdhiShThAnasya chetanasya bhogAdiprasakteruktatvAt.h | nanvayaM niradhiShThAnatvahetuH karturvipakShAtkulAlAdirvAkartuH sapakShAdghaTAderapi vyAvR^ittatvAdasAdhAraNaH | maivam.h | gaganAdau sapakShe vR^itteH | 
nanvidaM sUtradvayaM vyutkrameNa kuto vyAkhyAtam.h | sambandhAnupapattyadhiShThAnAnAnupapattyorubhayorapi parihAraH karaNavachchedityanena nirasyata iti j~nApanArtham.h | yadi khalu yathAkramameva vyAkhyAyeta | tadA sannihitAdhiShThAnAnupapattiparihAranirAsakamevedaM j~nAyeta | vyutkrameNa tu ubhayamadhye vyAkhyAne satyubhayasambandhi vij~nAyata iti | ata eva bhAShye.adhiShThAnAdirUpamityuktamatra tu dehAdivaditi |
nanu yuktaM kulAlasyAdhiShThAnasApekShatvaM sharIritvam.h | sharIraM hi gurutvAtprasaktapatanaM tatpratibandhAya sparshavadadhiShThAnamapekShate | anavasthitasharIrasya kartR^itvAyogAt.h | Ishvarasya tu sharIravidhurasya kimadhiShThAnameva | ihedaM jAtamityadivyavahArastu gaganAdikamAshrityopapatsyata ityata Aha- adehashchediti ||
sadetyanena vyAptimupapAdayati | ata eva shilAkAShThAdivadityanekadR^iShyAntopAdAnam.h | tathAcha kutaH sAvarj~nam.h | kutashcha sarvakartR^itvamiti bhAvaH | syAdetat.h | na sarvathA sadAshivaH asharIraH | kintu lIlayA sharIrANyapi gR^ihNAti | tato nAyaM doShaH | nacha bhogAdiprAptiH | lIlayA gR^ihItasya vigrahasya tadahetutvAdityata Aha- dehI chediti ||
antavAnmaraNavAnsyAt.h | upalakShaNaM chaitat.h | duHkhAdimAMshcha syAdityapi draShyavyam.h | nanvasau vigraho na taddheturityuktam.h | maivam.h | sharIraM na bhogAyatanaM chetyasya vyAhatatvAt.h | sharIratvenaiva tadanumAnAchcha | tadidamAha- eveti || etena "antavattmasarvaj~natA vA' iti sUtraM vyAkhyAtaM bhavati | pAThakramAdarthakramo garIyAnityato vyutkrameNa vyAkhyAnam.h | 
nanvevaM shivasya jagatkAraNatvamapAkurvatAM ko.abhiprAyaH | kimakartR^ikamevedaM vishvamiti | kiMvA viShNukartR^ikamiti | nAdyaH | kAryasyAkartR^ikatve virodhAt.h | apasiddhAntaprasakteshcha | na dvitIyaH | viShNAvapi kartaryabhyupagamyamAne doShANAmeShAM samAnatvena (sva)vyAhatatvAt.h | tathAhi yaduktamasAmaJNjasyaM shivasya tattAvadviShNAvapi samam.h | "janitota viShNoH' ityAdau janmAdidoShashravaNAt.h | sambandhAnupapattyAdikaM tu sphuTamevetyata Aha- nacheti ||
etadakhilaM doShajAtaM, viShNAvapi vishvasya kartaryabhyupagate samAnamiti na vAchyam.h | kutaH | shrutyaiva sakaladoShaparihAreNa viShNorvishvakAraNatvasya pratipAditatvAt.h |
nanu pashupaterapyevamAgamairanumAnaishcha jagatkAraNatA pratipAditaiva | tataH ko visheSha ityata Aha- shrutIti ||
pAshupatAdito.api shrutInAM prAmANyasya gurutvAt.h | etaduktaM bhavati | pAshupatAdikaM hi shive jagatkartari sarvaj~ne siddhe tatpraNItatvena pramANatvena nishchIyeta | nishchite cha tatprAmANye shivasyaivaMvidhasya siddhirityanyonyAshrayatA duravadhAraNaprAmANyam.h | anyataH shivasyaivaMvidhatAsiddhAvalamanena | na chAnyattAdR^ishaM pramANamasti | anumAnAnAM dUShitatvAt.h | nachaivaM shrutiprAmANyam.h | apauruSheyatvena karaNadoShANAM bAdhakapratyayasya chAbhAve sati tasya niShkampameva svato nishchitatvAt.h | ato nishchitapramANabhAvayA shrutyA vidhUtAvadyagandhaM viShNorjagatkAraNatvaM siddhayatyeveti | 
kAstAH shrutaya ityatastA udAharati- mana iti ||

prabhuH sUtrakAraH, anena vyAchikhyAsitatayA buddhisannihitena tR^itIyena pAdena vaidikAnAM vachanAnAM parasparaM avirodhaM virodhAbhAvaM, darshayatIti pratipAdyakathanam.h | asyAntarbhAvalakShaNAM saN^gatiM darshayitumuktam.h- asheSheti || asheShAshcha te samAmnAyavirodhAshcheti vigrahaH | kariShyan.h ityadhyAyopakramasamayApekShayA | sUtrakR^itA khalu sarvAnapi vedavirodhAnparihartuM dvitIyo.ayamadhyAya ArabdhaH | vaidikAnAM vachanAnAM parasparavirodho.api tadantarbhUta evetyatastadapAkaraNamiha saN^gatameveti | AnantaryalakShaNAM saN^gatiM darshayitumathetyuktam.h | avasaraprAptau prAdhAnyAdyuktivirodhaparihArasya prAthamye tatprapaJNchAtmakatvena samayavirodhaparihArasya tadAnantarye sati shrutInAM parasparavirodhaparihArasya bhavatyayamavasara iti |

"eSha brahmaiSha prajApatirindraH' ityAdinA vishvaprapaJNchamanUdya sarvaM tatpraj~nAnetramiti tasya praj~nAkhyabrahmanetR^ikatvamabhidhAya netR^inetavyabhAvasya kalpitatvAdityAshaN^kAnivR^ittyarthaM praj~nAnetro.aloka iti shrutyA muktAvapi jIvaparayorbhedo.abhidhIyate.aloko mukto.api praj~nAnetro brahmanetR^ika iti | nIyate.aneneti netram.h | dAmnItyadisUtrAt.h | praj~nA cha brahma | "praj~nA pratiShThA praj~nAnaM brahma' iti vAkyasheShAt.h | nachAtra loka iti padaM Chedyam.h | janabhuvanadeharUpasya lokasya prAgeva brahmanetR^ikatvasyoktatvena punaruktiprasaN^gAt.h | nacha netR^inetavyayorabhedaH kvachidasti | nachAvAntaramuktiviShayeyaM shrutiH | tatra lokAtItatA.ayogAt.h | dehendriyAdivaikalyaM khalvalokatvam.h | paramamuktau chAnuvartamAno bhedo nAvidyAkalpito bhavitumarhatyatiprasaN^gAditi |

"R^ichAM tvaH poShamAste pupuShvAngAyatraM tvo gAyati shakvarIShu | brahmA tvo vadati jAtavidyAM yaj~nasya mAtrAM vimimIta u tva' iti mantrasyAyamarthaH | muktisthAne tvaH kashchid.h brahmA R^ichAM poShaM pupuShpvAnAste R^ichaH puShyAH kurvannAste | tvo brahmA shakvarIShu R^ikShvArUDhaM gAyatraM sAma gAyati | tvo brahmA jAtavidyAM pauruSheyavidyAM vadati | tvo brahmA yaj~nasya viShNormAtrAmaMshameva vimimIte dhyAyatIti | atrApi bhedaH sphuTa evAvabhAsate | brahmabAhulyashravaNAtparamamokShatvaM cha | nachAsya R^itvigviShayatvam.h | brahmaNo jAtavidyAvAditvasyAprasiddhatvAt.h | chaturNAmapi pAdAnAM hotrAdibhinnaviShayatve tR^itIyapAde tva iti cha vyarthaM syAt.h | chashabdo vAkyasheShasamuchchaye |

duHkhAdIMshcha parityajyetyanena "jyotirmayeShu deheShu svechChayA vishvamokShiNaH | bhuJNjate susukhAnyeva na duHkhAdInkadAchana' ityAdi(kaM) brahmavaivartavAkyaM gR^ihyate | atra bahuvachanena bhedo duHkhAdyabhAvena paramamuktitvaM chAva(sIyate)bhAsate |

bhedo mithyetyetAvatyukte chandrabhedAdinA siddhasAdhanaM syAdityota vimata ityuktam.h | jIvabrahmaNorbheda iti yAvat.h | stambhakumbhAdibhedasya pakShatulyatvAnna tatra bhedatvahetorvyabhichAraH shaN^kanIya iti j~nApanArthaM vA | yAvAnkashchidvimato bhedaH sa sarvo.apIti | bhedagrahaNaM (vi)spaShyArtham.h | sAdhyAvadhAraNenAsiddhayAdyAbhAsoddhAraM sUchayati | bhedamithyAtvasiddhAvabheda eva vAstavaH siddhayatIti bhAvaH | 
dUShayituM pR^ichChati- sAdhyeti ||
ayaM jIvabrahmabhedasya mithyAtvalakShaNaH | sanniti svamatAnusAreNa | nanu mithyAtvaM sachchettadyasya tadapi satsyAt.h | nahi sambhavati nAsti dharmI dharmashchAstIti | tathAcha vaiparI(tyameva)tyam.h | maivam.h | mithyAtvaM khalvatyantAbhAvapratiyogitvaM tachcha buddhidvAreNaiva | atyantAsato.api pratItiraN^gIkriyate | tathAcha mithyAtvamastItyasya tatpratiyogiko.atyantAbhAvaH sannityarthaH | nachAtra ko.api virodhaH | 
asanveti mAdhyamikamatAnurodhena | nahi prativAdinyAshvAso.asti | yenAsau svamatamatipa(tI)tya na vadediti nishchinumaH |

yadyayaM sAdhyadharmaH sannityuchyate tadA mAyAvAdino.apasiddhAntaH syAt.h | nahi jIvabrahmaNobharedasya mithyAtvaM brahma, yena tasya sattve.api sadadvaitavAdino nApasiddhAntaH syAt.h | brahmaNo nirvikalpakatvAt.h | 
dvitIye doShamAha- sa eveti ||
apasiddhAnta eva | mithyAtvasyAsattve (api) sattvameva jIvabrahmabhedasya syAt.h | nachAsat.h pramANaviShaya iti teShAM pakShaH | anena sadasattvapakSho.api nirasto veditavyaH | antimamapAkaroti- nobhayaM chediti |
tadubhayavilakShaNatvaM cha jIvabrahmabhedamithyAtve.anyatra vA kvApi na siddham.h | 
nanvanena kimuktaM syAt.h | aprasiddhavisheShaNatvamiti chenna | sadasadvailakShaNyasya pakShavisheShaNatvAbhAvAt.h | mithyAtvameva pakShavisheShaNamupanyastaM taddharma eva sadasadvailakShaNyam.h | nacha vimataM buddhimatkartR^ipUrvakamitivadvisheShaNenApi prasiddhena bhAvyamiti vAchyam.h | vaiShamyAt.h | yaddhi vyApakakoTiniviShyaM vivAdapadaM cha tasya prasiddhatA.avashyambhAvinI | anyathA vyAptigrahaNapakSha(tva)yorasambhavAt.h | asti cha buddhimattvasyApi vyApakoTi(Tau) niveshAdi na tu sadasadvailakShaNyasyeti | uchyate | yo hyarthaH pramANasAdhyaH sa sambhAvitaprakAreShvanyatamaprakAravAnupalabdhaH | idaM cha jIvabrahmabhedasya mithyAtvaM na sadAdiprakAravadaN^gIkartuM shakyaM prakAratrayasyApasiddhAntaparAhatatvAt.h | chatutharsyAprAmANikatvAt.h | na hyaprAmANikena prakAreNa prakAravatkiJNchidbhavati | ato vyApakAnupalabdhibAdhitaM jIvabrahmaNobharedasya mithyAtvaM na sAdhayituM shakyamiti samudAyArtho 
vivakShita iti na kAchidanupapattiH | anenaivAbhiprAyeNa TIkA.api netavyeti |
dUShaNAntaramAha- iti mAnasyeti ||
mIyata iti mAnam.h | kR^ityalluTo bahulamiti vachanAt.h | mithyAshabdArthaM vikalpyApyevaM dUShaNamabhidhAnIyamityarthaH | tathAhi | kiM mithyetyasattvamuchyate | kiMvA.anirvAchyatvam.h | Adye.apasiddhAntaH | dvitIye.aprasiddhavisheShaNatA pakShasyeti | sattvAbhAvo mithyApadArtha iti chenna | tasyaivAsattva(shabdArtha)padArthatvenApasiddhAntAnistArAditi |
doShAntaramAha- itIti || mAnasya liN^gasya | bhedatvaheturapi sannasanvA sadasanvA anirvAchyo veti vikalpyAdye.advaitavAdino.asiddhiH | dR^iShyAntasya sAdhanavikalaH | dvitIyatR^itIyayordvayorapi | chaturthe dvaitavAdina iti dUShaNamabhidhAtavyamityarthaH | nacha sadasadAdau bhedatvasAmAnyamasti | yena dhUmavattvavadayaM hetuH syAt.h |
jIvo brahmaNo na bhidyate AtmatvAdbrahmavadityAdAvanumAnAntare.apyevameva vikalpya dUShaNAntaramabhidhAtavyamityAha- iti mAnasyeti || yadvA.advaitavAdiprayukteShu viruddhaviShayeShu sarveShvapi anumAneShvevaM sAdhyaM hetuM cha vikalpya doSho vaktavya ityatidishati- itIti ||
na siddhaM tadityayuktam.h | pakShIkR^ite bhede vA prapaJNche vA.avidyAyAM vA shaktirajatAdau vA.anirvachanIyatvasya pramANena sAdhayituM shakyatvAdityata Aha- nacheti ||
yadA bhedamithyAtvasya sattvAdivikalpena dUShaNAbhidhAnaM tadAntarashabdo visheShavachanaH | yadA tu mithyAshabdA(rthaM)rthavika(lpya)lpena dUShaNAbhidhAnaM tadAnyanmAnaM mAnAntaram.h | etat.h anirvAchyatvam.h | kvachit.h ityuktasthaleShu |
tatkathamiti chedittham.h | kasyachitpadArthasyAnirvAchyatve pratyakShaM vA pramANamuchyate anumAnaM vA.a.agamo vA.arthApattirvopamAnaM vA.abhAvo veti manasi vikalpAnnidhAya parAN^gIkAraprAchuryAnurodhenAnumAnaM tAvadapAkaroti- anumAnena chediti ||
vimatamanirvAchyaM bAdhyatvAdityAdyanumAnena shuktirajatAderanirvAchyatvaM sAdhyate chedanavasthA bhaviShyati | katham.h | saiva hi aprasiddhavisheShaNatAparihArArthAnumAnaparamparAdvArikA prasiddhaivetyarthaH | yadatra vaktavyaM tatprathamasUtra evAsmAbhirabhihitam.h |
AgamamapAkaroti- nacheti ||
tadartho.anirvachanIyArthaH | anupalambhAditi bhAvaH | nanu kathaM nAsti | nAsadAsInnosadAsIttadAnImityAgamasya vidyamAnatvAdityata Aha- nAsaditi ||
ityAgama iti sheShaH | tat.h anirvAchyaM vastu | ayaM bhAvaH | padasamanvayabalena pratItaH padArthasaMsargo hi vAkyArtho nAparaH | anyathA.arthApattyAderapyAgamAntarbhAvaprasaN^gAt.h | atra cha pralaye sadAdyabhAvamAtraM vAkyAtpratIyate na punaranirvAchyaM vastu | tato nAyamAgamo.anirvAchyArtha iti | mA bhUdayamAgamo.anirvachanIyArthaH | tathA.apyetadvachanabalenAnirvachanIyArthaH setsyati | tathAhi | atra tAvatpralaye sadasadabhAva; pratipAdyate | tatsAmarthyAttadA vidyamAnasyArthasya sattvAsattvapratiShedhAvagatau parisheShAdanirvAchyatvAvagateH | nacha tadA vastumAtrAbhAvaH | punaH sR^iShyayanupapatteH | abhAvasyAN^gIkAryatvAchcha |

nacha vAchyaM yadyapi pralaye paramAtmA vidyata eva | tathA.api tama AsIdityadisannihitavAkyAttamo.avidyAkhyaM buddhisannihitamiti tadupaktAyAM buddhau parisheShapramANamapi tamasa eva anivarAchyatAmAdhAsyatIti | AnIdavAtamiti vAkyena brahmaNo.api buddhisannidhAnAt.h | satyaM j~nAnamiti tasya satyatvAvagamAdapavAda iti chenna | AsIditi tamaso.api sattvAvagamAdapavAdaH syAt.h | sAMvyAvahArikaM sattvaM taditi chet.h | brahmaNo.api tathA kinna syAt.h | kiJNchAsminvyAkhyAne tadAnImiti vyarthaM sadA tamaso.anirvAchyatvAt.h | anyaparaM vAkyamiti chet.h | tathA.apyasannAsIditi vyarthameva | prAptyabhAvAt.h |

nanu jIvaM pakShIkR^ityeshvarAbhedasAdhane bhavedeyaM pratyakShavirodhaH | nachaivamanumIyate | kintvIshvaraM pakShIkR^itya jIvAbheda ityata Aha- anubhUtAddhIti ||naIshvaraM pakShIkurvatA hi tatsiddhiravashyaM vaktavyA | nacha pratyakShAdinA sa siddhayatIti shrutireva tadgrAhikA grAhyA | eShA(hi) cha dharmipramANabhUtA "yaH sarvaj~naH' satyAdikA shrutiH anumIshvaramalpaj~natvAdinA.anubhUtAjjIvAdbhedenavadati | tasmAtpratyakShabAdhAbhAve.apyupajIvyashrutivirodhena kAlAtyayApadiShyatA duShpariharaiva | sadAvagatAlpaj~natvAdimaJNjIrasvarUpaM prati sArvaj~nAdimadIshvarasvarUpaM pratipAdayantI shrutistatastaM bhinnameva pratipAdayati | anubhavasyApalapitumashakyatvAt.h | anenaivobhayapakShIkAro.api parAstaH | upajIvyapratyakShashrutibAdhitatvAditi |
