tushabdo visheShArthaH | duShyaM hyanumAnamaprA(Nameva bha)NaM bhavati | shrutestu pratItArthaprachyAvanamAtramiti | aikyaM jIveshvarayoH | shrutyA hi yadi jIvamanUdya tasyeshvaraikyaM bodhyate tadA jIvagrAhakaM sAkShipratyakShamupajIvyaM syAt.h | tachcha bhedagrAhakamityuktamityupajIvyavirodhaH | yadi cheshvarAnuvAdena tasya jIvAbhedo vidhIyate tadA yaH sarvaj~na ityAdikaM shrutyantaramevopajIvyaM bhavet.h | tachcha bhedagrAhakamityuktatvAdupajIvyavirodha eva | yadi chobhayAnuvAdenAbhedamAtrabodhyaM tadobhayamupajIvyamityupajIvyapramANavirodhaH sphuTa eva | yadyapyetatsarvaM prathamasUtra evoktam.h | tathA.api prapaJNchanAtharM punarArabhyata ityadoShaH |
nanUpajIvyavirodhenopajIvakaM bAdhyata ityatra kiM niyAmakam.h | yena pratyakShAgamavirodhAdanumAnAgamayoraprAmANyamuktam.h | uchyate | iha hi bhedAbhedaviShayorupajIvyopajIvakayorubhayorapi prAmANyameva vA.aprAmANyameva vA | ekasya prAmANyamaparasyAprAmANyaM vA | tatrApyupajIvakasya prAmANyamupajIvyasyAprAmANyaM vA | upajIvyasya prAmANyamupajIvakasyAprAmANyamiti pakShAH sambhavati | tatra na tAvatprathamaH | viruddhayoH prAmANyAnupapatteH | upapattau vA vastuno dvarUpyApatteH | bhrAntibAdhavyavasthA.abhAvaprasaN^gAchcha | nacha bhedAbhedAbhyAmupapattiH | nirAkariShyamANatvAt.h | asArvatrikatvAchcha | nachAnaikAntavAdena nistAraH | dvayorapi sAvadhAraNatvAsambhavAt.h | nApi dvitIyaH vastuno nissvabhAvatvApatteH | nachAnirvAchyatAsvIkAreNa nirvAhaH | brahmaNyapi sambhavAditi pakShadvayamatisphuTadoShatvAdanirAkR^itya tR^itIyaM dUShayati- aprAmANyamiti ||
bhedavAchakasyAgamasyetyupalakShaNam.h | bhedagrAhiNaH pratyakShasyetyapi draShyavyam.h | evaM tadA sa evetyatrApi vyAkhyAtatvAt.h | dharmiNo jIvasyeshvarasya cha | itishabdo.adhyAhAryaH | kathaM bodhya iti sheShaH | idamuktaM bhavati | yadyaj~nAnAdivishiShyasya jIvasya sArvaj~nAdivishiShyasya paramAtmano grAhakaM pratyakShamAgamavAkyaM vA.aprAmANyaM syAt.h | tadA jIveshvarayorasiddhau tattvamasyAdyAgamairanumAnaishcha tadabhedabodhanaM na syAt.h | nirviShayatvAt.h | tathAcha kasya virodhAtpratyakShAderaprAmANyaM syAt.h | j~nApakashchAyamartho na kArakaH | akhaNDArthabodhanamapi laukikavAkyanyAyamanusR^itya pashchAllakShaNayA pareNAbhyupagatam.h | na punarevameva | alaukikaprakArasya bodhAnaN^gatvAt.h | tasmAdupajIvakavirodhenopajIvyasyAprAmANyAyogAtparisheShatashchaturthaprakAra eva cha siddhayatIti |
bhavedevopajIvakAdupajIvyaM balavattadvirodhe chopajIvakasyAprAmANyam.h | kinnAmAsti tatra visheShaH | anekaprakAro hyupajIvyopajIvakabhAvaH | kvachiddharmigrAhaka(tayeti)tvena | kvachitsAdhyagrAhakatayA | kvachittadgrahaNopayuktatayA | kvApi svarUpagrahaNena | kutrachitprAmANyopapAdanena | kvachidvayAptyAdyaN^gapratipAdakatveneti | tatra sarvatropajIvyaviruddhamupajIvakaM bAdhyata eva | AshrayAdihInasyotthAnavirahApatteH | yatra punaH pratiShedhakasyopajIvakasya pratiShedhyasamarpakamupajIvyaM bhavati | tadA nAyaM nyAyaH | chopajIvakenaivopajIvyasya bAdhaH | niShedhArthameva tena tadupajIvanAt.h | dR^iShyaM hIdaM rajatamiti j~nAnasya nedaM rajatamiti j~nAnena bAdhyatvAt.h | tadihApi yaduktamabhedapramANayoranumAnAgamayorupajIvyAbhyAM pratyakShAgamAbhyAM virodhAdaprAmANyamiti tadayuktam.h | pratyakShAgamayoranumAnAgamau prati niShedhyasamarpakatayopajIvyatvAt.h | bhedaniShedho hi na tatprAptiM sambhavati | tenAtropajIvakavirodhinorupajIvyayoH pratyakShAgamayorevAprAmANyamuchitamityato yaH sarvaj~na ityAderAgamasya tAvadaprAmANyamapAkaroti- aprAmANyamiti ||
bhedavAchakasya bhedakasArvaj~nAdivishiShyaparamAtmapratipAdakasyAgamasya | etaduktaM bhavati | samutthAnavatA khalvanumAnenAgamena vA virodhinA yaH sarvaj~na ityAdyAgamasyAprAmANyasyeShyavyam.h | asyAprAmANye tvanumAnAderutthAnameva durlabham.h | dUre tadbAdhanam.h | paramAtmalakShaNasya dharmiNastadekagamyatvAt.h | nirAshrayasyAnumAnAdeH pravR^ittyanupapattiriti |
nanvevaM tarhi nedaM rajatamiti j~nAnavirodhena idaM rajatamita j~nAnasyAprAmANyaM na syAt.h | na na syAt.h | nahi nedaM rajatamiti j~nAnaM 
rajatAvishiShyaM vastu dharmIkR^ityotpadyate kintu svarUpamAtram.h | sarvamapi hi, j~nAnaM dharmiNi pramANaM prakAre tu viparyayaH  (dharmiNyabhrAntamakhilaM j~nAnamichChanti vAdinaH | viparyayaM prakAre tu vadanti rajatAdike' iti sAyaNashikShAbhAShye vArtikasAravachanam.h | atrApi tR^itIyAdhyAye chatutharpAde "tathA.anyepyAhuH sarvaM j~nAnaM dharmiNi pramANaM prakAre tu viparyaya iti) | tadatrApIdaM rajatamiti j~nAnamidamaMshe pramANamiti tatsiddhamidamAkAramAshritya pravR^ittena bAdhakapratyayena virodhAdrajatAMshe pUrvaj~nAnasyAprAmANyaM yujyata eva |
nanvanenaiva nyAyenAbhedAnumAnAgamavirodhena yaH sarvaj~na ityAdishruteraprAmANyaM shakyopapAdanam.h | iyamapi shrutirbrahmasvarUpamAtre pramANamiti tanmAtramupajIvyAnumAnAgamAbhyAM sArvaj~nAdibhedakadharmavaishiShyayAMshe.apramANIkariShyate | tathAcha yaddharmigrAhakaM na tadvirodho.anumAnAdeH | yachcha virodhi na taddharmipramAramityata Aha- yaditi ||
yachChativAkyaM brahmasvarUpagrahaNArthaM mAnamaN^gIkriyate | taddharme sArvaj~nAdidharmavaishiShyayAkAre kathaM na mAnaM bhavet.h | 
ayamabhisandhiH | shuktirajatAdij~nAnaM hIdamaMshe pramANaM rajatavaishiShyayAMshe tvapramANamiti yuktam.h | vaishiShyayAMshasya bAdhakapramANaviruddhatvAt.h | idamAkArasyottaratrApyanuvR^itteH | idaM na rajatamiti bAdhakaj~nAnamutpadyate na punarnedaM rajataM cheti | nachAyamatra nyAyaH | svarUpavadvishiShyAMshe.api bAdhakAbhAvAt.h | nachAbhedAnumAnAgamau bAdhakau | anyonyAshrayatvAt.h | bAdhitatvena shruteraprAmANye satyupajIvyavirodharahitasyAnumAnAderbAdhakatvaM sati cha tasmiMstadvirodhinyAH shruteraprAmANyamiti |
kathaM chAnumAnAdeH shrutibAdhakatvam.h | natAvadvirodhitvamAtreNa | vaiparItyasyApi suvachatvAt.h | nApi virodhyuttaraj~nAnatvena shuktirUpyamiti j~nAnAnantaraM rajatamidamiti j~nAnasya darshanAt.h | anuttaravirodhij~nAnaM bAdhakamidaM tu sottaramityapi na | kadAchidanuttarasyApi rajataj~nAnasya sambhavAt.h | kintu yAvachChakti parIkShitamuttaraM virodhyaparIkShitasya pUrvasya bAdhakaM bhavati | nachaivamatrAstIti | 
na kevalaM bAdhakAbhAvasAmyAdayaM vibhAgo na yuktaH kiM tarhItyata Aha- eketi ||
ekavidhamevedaM yaH sarvaj~na ityAdishrutijanitaM vij~nAnaM, na punaH shuktirajatAdij~nAnamiva svarUpamAtre pramANaM vishiShyAkAre tvapramANamityanekavidhamityevaM parIkShAsahakR^itasAkShirUpavij~naptyA.apIdaM j~nAnadvayaM dharmadharmidvayagarbhaM vishiShyAkAraM pratyapi mAnaM bhavatyeva | vakShyate chAyamarthaH prapaJNchena | yadvA dvayaM pratItidvayaM svarUpavaddharme.apIti yojyam.h | 
athavA yaH sarvaj~na ityAdishruterbrahmasvarUpamAtre prAmANyamaprAmANyaM tu sArvaj~nAdivishiShyAkAra iti vadataH ko.abhiprAyaH | kiM shuktirajatAdij~nAnamivaikamevedaM j~nAnaM viShayabhedena pramANamapramANaM cheti | kiMvA j~nAnadvayametat.h tatraikaM pramANamaparaM chApramANamiti | AdyaM dUShayati- yaditi || pUrva evAbhiprAyaH | dvitIyaM nirAkaroti- eketi | ekamevedaM vij~nAnamiti sAkShivij~naptyA nAnekatvaM kalpyamiti sheShaH | anyathA stambho.ayamityAdAvapi j~nAnadvayakalpanApattiH | tathAcha sAmAnAdhikaraNyaM na kenApi j~nAyeta | 
astu vedaM j~nAnadvayaM tathApi naikasyAprAmANyaM vaktuM shakyate | svarUpaj~nAnasyeva dharmaj~nAnasyApyabAdhitatvAdityAha- dvayamiti || j~nAnadvayamapItyarthaH | dharmaj~nAnamapIti(cha) vaktavye dvayamiti vachanaM nyAyasAmyasUchanArtham.h |
evaM bAdhAbhAvaparIkShitatvasAmye.api shrautamekaM j~nAnadvayaM vA.aN^gIkR^ityAMshataH prAmANyaprAmANye vadato.atiprasaN^gamAha- nachediti || tachChrautaM j~nAnaM dvayaM vishiShyAkAraM prati pramANaM na chettadA.atra viShaye ekaM svarUpAMshaM pratyapi pramANaM na bhavet.h | avisheShAt.h | tathAcha punaranAshrayayoranumAnAgAmayoranutthAnameva | yadvA tadvij~nAnamatra viShaye ekaM vishiShyAkAraM prati pramANaM chettadA dvayaM pratyapi no bhavet.h | vishiShyAkAravatsvarUpe.api pramANaM na bhavet.h | avisheShAditi yAvat.h | j~nAnadvayAN^gIkAravAde tvatra j~nAnadvaye tadvishiShyaviShayaM j~nAnaM pramANaM na chettarhi j~nAnadvayamapi pramANaM na bhavet.h | vishiShyaj~nAnamiva svarUpaj~nAnamapyapramANaM syAdavisheShAditi | 
evamabhedAnumAnAgamau prati yaH sarvaj~na iti shruterniShedhyasamarpakatvenopajIvyatvaM pratyuktam.h | tathA.api nAnumAnAgamayorupajIvyapramANavirodho.asti | yaH sarvaj~na ityAdishrutisiddhabrahmasvarUpamAtrAshrayaNena pravR^ittatvAt.h | nahi sArvaj~nAdivishiShyAkAramavalambyAnumAnAdinA pravartitavyamityatra niyAmakamasti | tato viruddhAkArasyAnupayogitayA.anupajIvanAdupajIvyasya cha svarUpamAtrasyAvirodhitvAnnopajIvyapramANavirodho.anumAnAdeH pramANavirodhastu kathaJNchitsyAdityAshaN^kAM pariharannupasaMharati- dharmIti ||
tushabdo visheShArthaH, pramANamAtravirodhAdvayavachChinatti | dharmigrAhiNyA shrutyA virodhaH | mAnasya abhedapramANasyAnumAnAgamarUpasya | ayamAshayaH | paramANavaH sAvayavA ityAderanumAnasya vAkyasya cha kathamupajIvyavirodhaH iti vaktavyam.h | 
paramANutvasyAnupayogino.anupajIvyatvaM kintu svarUpamAtrasyeti vaktuM shakyatvAt.h | naivaM yuktam.h | niravayatvAdinA vinA paramANordharmIkaraNAsambhavAt.h | svarUpamAtradharmIkaraNe siddhArthatApattiriti chet.h | samaM prakR^ite.api | nahi brahmApi sArvaj~nAdinA vinA shakyaM dharmIkartum.h | svarUpamAtradharmIkaraNe siddhasAdhanAt.h | Aropitena sArvaj~nAdinA vyAvR^ittasya dharmIkaraNe ko doShaH | yo.ayaM sthANuH sa puruSha itivaditi chenna | Aropitena niravayavatvAdinA vyAvR^ittasya tatrApi dharmIkaraNasambhavAt.h | niravayavatvAdigrAhakaM pramANatayA.avadhR^itam.h | nAropitaM iti chet.h | tulyamatrApi | shruterapi prAmANyanishchayAt.h | tadevaM pramANasiddhena niravayavatvAdinA vishiShyasyaiva yathA dharmIkaraNaM tathA.atrApi sAvarj~nAdinA pAramArthikenaiva vishiShyasyaiva dharmIkaraNamityato dharmigrAhakavirodho duShparihara iti | 
syAdetat.h | yathA khalvabhedapramANayoranumAnAgamayorupajIvyavirodhAnnAbhedasAdhakatvaM tathodAhR^itAyA bhinno.achintya ityAdibhedashruterapyupajIvyavirodhAnna bhedasAdhakatvaM sambhavati | tAdAtmyapratiyogikaH pratiShedho hi bhedo nAma | nachAprApte tAdAtmye tatpratiShedhabodhanaM yuktamityabhedaprApakaM pramANamupajIvya pravR^ittA bhedashrutiH kathaM nopajIvyaviruddhA | kiJNcha nirbhedaM svarUpamAshritya tasya bhedo bodhanIyaH | tathAcha kathaM nopajIvyavirodhaH | yathoktam.h "abhedaM nollikhantI dhIrna bhedollekhanakShamA | tathAchAdye pramA sA syAnnAntye svApekShyavaishasAt.h' ityata Aha- neti || 
hishabdo yuktisUchakaH | abheda iti tad.hgrAhakam.h | atra kvachiditi | dharmitvAdAvityarthaH | tadayamarthaH | bhedashruterhi na dharmisamarpakatvenAbhedaj~nAnopajIvakatvaM tAvat.h | jIveshvarasvarUpasyaiva dharmitvAt.h | nApi svarUpaprAmANyagrAhakatvena | pratyakSheNaiva tatsiddheH | ato niShedhyaprApakatayaiveti vaktavyam.h | nacha tadvirodho.aprAmANyamAvahati | niShedhashAstrApalApaprasaN^gAt.h | nacha pramANaprAptasyAyaM pratiShedhaH | kintu tattvamasyAdishrutitAtparyAparij~nAnaprAptasyaiva | yadapi nibharedaM svarUpamAdAya bhedo boddhavya iti tatrApi na yayorbhedo bodhanIyastayorabheda AshrayaNIyaH | kintu svagatabhedaM vastu dharmitayopAdAya tasyAntato bhedo bodhyate | ato jIveshabhedashrutestadabhedopajIvanAbhAvAdanapekShatvalakShaNAdbalAdyuktaM bhedasAdhakatvamiti sheShaH | 
kiJNcha tiShThatu tAvadyaH sarvaj~na ityAdishruterupajIvyatvam.h | tathA.apyabhedAnumAnAgamabAdhakatvaM bhavedeva | iyaM khalu shrutiH sArvaj~nAdivishiShyamIshvaraM pratipAdayantI na kiJNchidapekShate | anumAnAgamau tu sApekShau | sApekShanirapekShayoshcha nirapekShasya prAbalyAdityAshayavAnAha- nopajIvyo hIti ||
atra bhedAbhedapramANayormadhye | bhedashruteH bhedakadharmavishiShyadharmishruteH | abheda ityabhedapramANam.h | anapekShatvopalakShaNametat.h | ato balAdabhedapramANabAdhakatvamiti sheShaH | 
syAdetat.h | yaH sarvaj~na ityAdishrutirna jIvabhedakadharmavishiShyaM brahma pratipAdayati | kintvanuvadatyeva | ato nAnumAnAdestadbAdha ityata Aha- nacheti ||
upeyaM j~neyam.h | taditi sArvaj~nAdyupetam.h | kvachiditi bhrAntipratipannamapi na bhavatIti sUchayati | na tAvatsArvaj~nAdivishiShyaM brahma shrItivyatiriktapramANagamyam.h | shAstraikayonitvasya samarthitatvAt.h | nApi bhrAntipratipannam.h | kvachitpramitasyaivAnyatrAropAt.h | nacha pramANena bhrAntyA vA.aprAptasyAnuvAdaH sambhavati | ato neyaM shrutiranuvAdinI | kinnAma pratipAdayatyevoktarUpaM brahmeti |
nanu tathA.api nopajIvyapramANavirodho.anumAnAdeH | shrutyupajIvane hi saH syAt.h | na chaivam.h | tadvayatiriktapramANopajIvanAdityata Aha- nacheti || vastuvyavahito vahniradhUmasthale pratyakShAdyavedyo.api kvachiddeshe pratyakSheNAnumAnena vA.avagamyate | prAk.h patanotpatteragamyamapi gurutvaM kvachitkAle.anumAnena gamyate | nachaivaM brahma kvachinmAnAntaropeyam.h | yena tadupajIvyAnumAnAdipravR^ittiH syAt.h |
astu vA brahma pramANAntaravedyam.h | tathA.apyabhedAnumAnAderupajIvyapramANavirodho duShpariharaH | shrutivattasyApi pramANasya bhedapratyAyakatvAdityabhiprAyavAnAha- yeneti ||
upeyaM brahmeti sheShaH | tatkathamityata Aha- sa(sA)rvaj~neti ||
dharmAdikaM kasyachitpratyakShaM prameyatvAdghaTavadityAdikayA sA(sa)rvaj~nasAdhakatayA.anumayA | sarvakartR^itvAdyanumAnopalakShaNaM chaitat.h | eveti pratyakShaM vyAvartayati | kathaJNchanetyabhyupagamavAdo.ayamiti sUchayati | sarvaj~natvetyupalakShaNam.h | tayaivetyanvayaH | Ishvare tAvatpratyakShaM shaN^kArhameva na bhavati | ato.anumAnameva vaktavyam.h | pratipakShAdinA parAhatasyApi tasya kathaJNchichChaN^kArhatvAt.h | anumAnaM cha kiJNchitkenachidvishiShyameva pratipAdayati | natu niShkR^iShyaM vastu | nacha jIvAdisAdhAraNadharmavishiShyAtharsiddhAvIshvaraH sidhyati | tasmAdbhedakadharmavaishiShyayenaiva tatsiddhivarktavyA | tathAchAnumAnAderupajIvyavirodho vajralepAyitaH | yadyapyanumAnaM 
svataH shrutito durbalaM tathA.api upajIvyatayA bAdhakaM bhavatyeveti | 
tadaneneshvaragrAhikAyAH shruterbhedakadharmavishTi tasminprAmANyamupapAditam.h | idAnIM jIvagrAhakasya pratyakShasyeshvarabhedaka(vi)dharmiNi jIve prAmANyaM samarthyate | tathAhi | bhavatu shrutiraduHkhitvasArvaj~nAdimadIshvare pramANam.h | tathA.api nAbhedAnumAnAgamayorupajIvyapramANavirodhenAprAmANyam.h | duHkhitvAdirUpe hi jIvasya tAttvike sati tathA syAnna chaivam.h | ahaM duHkhItyAderanubhavasya mithyAnubhavatvAt.h | antaHkaraNagato hi duHkhAdiranarthaH svarUpato mithyAbhUto japAkusumAruNimeva sphaTike chaitanye chakAsti | nacha bhrAntipratipannena(nnabhe)bhedakena vastu bhidyata iti ata Aha- neti ||
kvApIti | sarvathetyarthaH | bhavedetadyadyahaM duHkhItyAdyanubhavo mithyAnubhavaH syAnna cha tathA | api tu pramANameva | yadyapi duHkhAdikamantaHkaraNagataM, tathA.api svarUpeNa sadeva | jIvAtmanashcha tadbhoktR^itvena tadvattvaM tAttvikameva | alpashaktitvapAratantAdikaM tu svarUpagatamevetyAshayaH | 
kuta ityata Aha- nahIti ||
tushabdo.avadhAraNe naiveti sambandhaH | asaJNjAtabAdhabhrameShu vyabhichAraparihArAya kvachidityuktam.h | nahi kadAchitkutrachitkashchinnAhaM duHkhI kintvantaHkaraNagatenaiva mithyAduHkhena duHkhitayA.a.atmAnamamani(ShI)Shamiti bAdhakapratyayavAndR^ishyata ityarthaH | nanu "vimuktashcha vimuchyate' "tattvamasi' ityAdishrutirevAsyAnubhavasya bAdhikA.astIti kathaM na duHkhAnubhUtirbhrAntiH | atra hi duHkhAdyupaplavarahitamevAsyAtmanastAttvikaM rUpamiti pratipAdyata ityata Aha- yadIti ||
avasIyate shrutimAshrityeti sheShaH | kena kAraNena | bhrAntiH svarUpato.arthatashcha | gamyate abhyupagamyate | anubhavamAshrityeti sheShaH | idamuktaM bhavati | bhavedeShA shrutirasyAnubhavasya bAdhikA | yadi nishchitapramANabhAvA bhavet.h | nacha tathA | dharmigrAhakAnubhavavirodhenAsmAbhiHtadaprAmANyasya pratipAdyamAnatvAt.h | parasya cha tatparihArAyAdyApi samudyatatvAt.h | tathAcha sati shrutiprAmANyanishchaye.anubhavasya bhrAntitvaM tasmiMshcha sati shrutiprAmANyanishchaya iti parasparAshrayatvaprasaN^gaH | nanvanubhavavirodhena shrutyaprAmANyAbhidhAne.api samAnametat.h | na samAnam.h | anubhavasyAnapekShatvAt.h shrutestadapekShatvAt.h | anyathA sarvatra dharmigrAhakavirodhochChedApa(tte)ttiriti | 
nanu tarhi nedaM rajatamityasyApi rajatamidamiti j~nAnaM prati bAdhakatvamayuktaM syAt.h | na syAt.h | nedaM rajatamiti j~nAnaprAmANyasya sAkShiNA parIkShayA nishchitatvAt.h | idaM rajatamiti j~nAnasya tadabhAvAt.h | parIkShitaprAmANyenopajIvakenopajIvyasyAtathAbhUtasya bAdhopagamAt.h | upajIvyopajIvakanyAyasya tadanyaviShayatvAt.h | prAmANyasandehe khalu nyAyAnusaraNam.h | nishchite tu prAmANye kimanena | vakShyati chaitadAchAryaH | evaM tarhi shruterapi prAmANyaM parIkShAsahakR^itena sAkShiNA nishchitamityanubhavabAdhakatvamupapatsyata ityAshayavAnAshaN^kate- shrutIti ||
svarUpamarthashcheti vivakShAbhedena prAmANyamevoktam.h | jIvasya nirduHkhabrahmAtmatApratipAdakashrutisvarUpamasyAH shruteH so.artha ityubhayatra phalato.arthabhedAbhAvAt.h | etadeva hi prAmANyamapi | mAnena sAkShiNA | pariharati- tachchediti ||
ta ityavyayaM tR^itIyArthe | te mata ityadhyAhAro vA | kiM kinnimittam.h | duHkhAnubhave bhrama iti | duHkhAnubhavasya bhramatvamiti(iti) yAvat.h | aN^gIkriyata iti sheShaH | tat.h sAkShilakShaNaM mAnaM duHkhAnubhavaviShaye bhramaH kuto.aN^gIkriyata iti vA | etaduktaM bhavati | sAkShiNA shrutiprAmANyaM nishchitamiti na pareNAN^gIkartuM shakyate | tathA sati tatprAmANyasyAN^gIkartavyatvaprasaN^gAt.h | iShyate taditi chenna | tathA satyahaM duHkhIti duHkhAdiviShayo.api sa eveti tatrApi tasya prAmANyameva grAhyaM syAnna bhramatvam.h | nachet.h shrutiprAmANyagrahaNe.api bhramaH syAditi | JOSHI-10
nvekatra prAmANye viShayAntare.api prAmANyena bhAvyaM tatrAprAmANye chAnyatrApi aprAmANyena bhavitavyamiti kuta etat.h | mA hi bhUdekasya chakShurAderayaM niyama ityata Aha- nacheti || 
bhededevaikasyApi kvachitprAmANye paratrAprAmANyam.h | kAraNavisheShAt.h | sa chotpattau doSho j~naptau bAdhaH | doSho.api bAdhonneya eva | yathoktam.h | "balavatpramANatashchaiva j~neyA doShA na chAnyathA' iti | tato bAdha eva visheShaH | nacha duHkhAdiviShayasya sAkShyanubhavasya bAdharUpo visheSho.asti | yenAsau shrutiprAmANye pramANabhUto.api duHkhAdau bhramaH syAt.h | yat.h yasmAdevaM tat.h tasmAt.h shrutiprAmANyamiva tat.h Atmano duHkhitvAdikamapyabAdhitameva satyamevAN^gIkAyarmiti | yadvA yadyasmAdevaM ta(tta)smAtkiM duHkhAnubhave bhrama iti pUrve(Naiva)Na sambandhaH | 
nanvetat.h shrutiprAmANyaM duHkhAdikaM cha sAkShigR^ihItameva | nachobhayatra prAmANyaM sAkShiNo yuktam.h | parasparavirodhAt.h | tata 
ekatrAprAmANyAvashyambhAve duHkhAdAveva taditi grAhyam.h | shrutiprAmANyasyApauruSheyatvAdiparIkShAsahakR^itena gR^ihItatvAt.h | ato mithyaiva duHkhitvAdikamita chenna | duHkhAdAvapi sajAtIyavijAtIyasaMvAdarUpaparIkShAsadbhAvAt.h | evaM tarhi sandehAnna duHkhAdisatyatAnishchayo bhavatAM yukta iti na shruteranubhavabAdho vaktuM shakyata ityata Aha- abAdhitameveti ||
tad.h duHkhaM satyamevetyavadhArayato.ayamabhisandhiH | satyam.h | shrutiprAmANyaM duHkhAdikaM cha sAkShigR^ihItameva | nachaikatrApi bAdhakamastItyubhayamapi pramANaM sAkShI | nacha virodhaH | advaitasattAmantareNApi shrutiprAmANyasattAyAH sambhavAt.h | nahyapauruSheyatvAdiyuktayo viShayavisheShaniyataprAmANyanishchaye (sAkShiNaH) sAchivyamAcharanti | kintu prAmANyamAtranishchaye | upakramAdyAstu tatra tatrAbhAsIkR^itA eva | nacha duHkhasattAmantareNa tatra prAmANyasya sambhavo.asti | nacha duHkhasattayA shrutiprAmANyamAtrasya virodho.asti | viShayAntare.api tasya sambhavAt.h | ataH satyameva duHkhAdikamiti |
shrutiranubhavasya bAdhikA na bhavati | kintu dharmigrAhakatayA prabalenAnubhavenaiva bAdhyata ityuktam.h | na kevalaM dhamirgrAhakatayA.anubhava(sya)prAbalyam.h | kinnAma shrutisvarUpaprAmANyagrAhakatvenApItyAshayavAnAha- shrutIti || artha ityarthavattvaM prAmANyamiti yAvat.h | svarUpataH prAmANyatashchAvasitA hi shrutirabhipretasiddhaye prayoktavyA nAnyathA | shratisvarUpaM tatprAmANyaM cha mAnenaiva sAkShilakShaNenAvasIyate nAnyena | yadyapi shratisvarUpaM shrotravedyaM tathA.api shrotrajanitatad.hvR^ittiprAmANyaM yAvanna sAkShiNA gR^ihyate tAvanna tat.h siddhayatItyataH shrutisvarUpAvasAyo.api sAkShiNyevAyatate | 
yadvA shrutishabde(nai)na tajjanitaM j~nAnamuchyate | tatra pR^ichChAmaH | tasya sAkShiNaH prAmANyaM bhavatA.apyabhyupagataM na veti | neti pakShe shrutisvarUpAdyasiddherna tadvirodhena duHkhAdyanubhavasya bhramatvaM vaktuM yuktam.h | AdyaM dUShayati- tachchediti || tat.h sAkShi(sva)rUpaM pramANaM tvayA gR^ihItaM chettadA duHkhAnubhavasya bhramatvaM kiM (kathaM) na kathaJNchit.h | shrutivirodhena khalu taduchyate | sA tu svarUpaprAmANyagrAhakatayopajIvyenAnubhavena bAdhitA kathaM tadbAdhanAya prabhavatIti | 
syAdetat.h | shrutisvarUpaprAmANyayoH sAkShiNaH prAmANyamaN^gIkriyate | duHkhAdau tu viShayAntare shrutivirodhenAprAmANyamAshrIyate | tatkathamuktadoSha ityata Aha- nacheti || bAdhasya bAdhakatvena abhimatAyAH shruteH visheSho bAdhyatayA.abhimatAtsAkShiNo.atishayo nAsti | asti choktavakShyamANarItyA sAkShiNa eva visheSha iti | shiShyaM spaShyam.h |
kiJNchAhaM duHkhItyAdisAkShiNo bhramatvaM vadanpraShyavyaH | kiM sarvatrApi sAkShiNo bhramatvamaN^gIkriyate | uta kvachitprAmANyamapi | Adye doShamAha- shrutisvarUpamiti ||
mAnena sAkShiNaiva | tathAcha tasya bhrAntitve tanna siddhayediti bhAvaH | paramArthato mA saitsIditi cha na vAchyam.h | tattvAvedakatvasyAN^gIkR^itatvAt.h | atha shrutisvarUpAdiviShaye tanmAnatvaM svIkriyata iti dvitIyamanUdyottaramAha- tachchediti || ekatra prAmANye paratrApi prAmANyamaN^gIkartavyamityetatkuta ityato.avisheShAdityAha- nacheti || pUrvavadvayAkhyAnam.h |
evaM sAkShiNaH pramANAntarasAdhAraNarUpatA(tva)mupetya bAdhakAbhAvenAhaM duHkhItyAdebhraMmatvaM nopapadyata ityuktam.h | idAnIM sAkShiNo yathArthatvaniyamAchcha na duHkhAdiviShaye bhramatvashaN^kopapadyate | kiM bAdhakagaveShaNAdinetyAshayavAnsAkShiNo yathArthatvaniyamaM vipakShe bAdhakena samarthayate- bAdha iti || 
anubhUte sAkShipratIte.athare yadi bAdhaH pravarteta sAkShI yadi kutrachidayathArthaH syAditi yAvat.h | ayathAtvarthasya bAdhonneyatvAdevamuktam.h | tadA kathaM stambho.ayaM kumbho.ayamiti padArthAnAM nirNaya Iyate upeyate |
etadeva prapaJNchayati- ko.apIti ||
bhramavAdinA sAkShiNaH kvachidbhramatvaM vadatA | (yadi) sAkShI kvachidayathArthaH syAttadA padArthanirNayo na syAdityarthaH | yathA.a.ahuranye.api | "j~nAnasya vyabhichAritve vishvAsaH kinnibandhanaH' iti |
nanu cha nirNayo nishchaya iti chAvadhAraNAtmakaM j~nAnamuchyate | tachcha stambhakumbhAdiShvartheShu tattatkAraNasAmagrIvashAdevotpadyate | nirNAyakAbhAvasahakR^itasamAnadharmadarshanAdinA hyanavadhAraNAtmakaM j~nAnaM saMshayapadavedanIyaM janyate | tadvilakShaNayA cha sAmagyrA avadhAraNaj~nAnam.h | tatra kaH sAkShiNo yAthArthyaniyamasyopayogaH | kiJNcha tadabhAvenApaneShyate | uchyate | na stambho.ayamityekAkArapratiniyataM j~nAnaM iha(hi) nirNayAdishabdairabhidhIyate | api tarhi tadanantarabhAvI vastutathAtvAshvAsaH | tathAhi | vaktAro bhavanti | stambha iti (cha) pratIyate bhavati chAyaM stambha iti vA vastutattvaM tu na vidma iti veti | tatkasya hetoH | ekAkArapratiniyateShvapi j~nAneSha keShAJNchidbhramatvasya keShAJNchidabhramatvasya bahulamupalabdhatvenedAnIM jAyamAnepye(Shve)kAkAraniyate j~nAne vastutathAtvavishvAsAyogAt.h | 
bhavatu vastutathAtvAshvAso vastudarshanapR^iShThabhAvI nirNayaH | so.api tasya dasharnasya bhramatvAbhramatvanirNayamevApekShate | yadi j~nAnaM bhramaH syAttadA vastvatathAbhUtamityavasIyate | yadi tvabhramastadA tathAbhUtamiti | evaMcha kiM sAkShiNo yAthArthyaniyamenopanIyate, kiMcha tasya bhramatvenApanIyata ityata Aha- bhramatvamiti ||
satyaM pratyayAnAM bhramatvAbhramatvanirNayAyatto vastunirNaya iti | saiva tatra pratyayeShvekasya stambhAdau puruShAdipratyayasya bhramatA.aparasya stambhAdipratyayasyAbhramatA cha kuto nirNetavyA na kuto.api | kuto yadA yataH | pratyayAnAM bhramatvamabhramatva cha anubhavopagaM sAkShiNaivAdhyavaseyamiti |

pratyayAnAM bhramatvamabhramatvaM tadavadhAraNopayuktaM cha sarvaM karaNadoShAdikaM sAkShiNA nishcheyam.h | anishchitasya bhramatvAdyavadhAraNAprasaN^gAt.h | sa chetsAkShI kvachit.h duShyaH ayathArthaH syAttadA kathaM kAraNadoShAderbhramatvAdervastutathAtvAdervA niNarya Iyate | etaduktaM bhavati | pratyayAnAM bhramatvAvadhAraNaM kA(ka)raNadoShAdyAyattaM tathA.api sAkShiNo yAthArthyaniyamAbhAve na siddhayet.h | nahi tatsvarUpeNopayuktam.h | atiprasaN^gAt.h | kintu nishchitameva tannishchayashcha sAkShAtkAraparamparayA vA sAkShiNyAyatate | sa hi kA(ka)raNadoShAdikaM svayameva (vA) tadgrAhakaprAmANyagrahaNena vA nishchitya bhramatvaM nishchinoti | tatashcha tasya kvachidayathArthatve.avishvasanIyatvApattyA na nirNayaH syAt.h | abhramatvanishchayastu na saMvAdAdhInaH | tathA satyanavasthAdidoShAH prAduShyurityuktam.h | kintu kevalasAkShiNyAyattaH | viparyayashaN^kAnirAse tu saMvAdasyAnupraveshaH | nacha saMvAdo.apyanishchito.aN^gam.h | tannishchayashcha sAkShyadhIna eva | tasya cha kvachidayathArthatve tadubhayanirNayo.api na bhavediti |

nishchityetyarthaH | cho.avadhAraNe | tAnsarvAnkA(ka)raNadoShA(dI)n.h UrIkR^itya vyavahAra pravartata iti gauNaM samAnakartR^ikatvam.h | yadvorIkR^itya kAraNatayopAdAya kAraNIkR^itveti vyAkhyeyam.h | tathAhi | idaM rajatamiti bhrAntyA pravR^ittaH kA(ka)raNadoShaM bAdhakapratyayaM (chA)vAvadhArya tasya j~nAnasya bhramatvaM nishchitya nedaM rajataM kintu shuktireveti vastu vyavasthApya jahAti | tathA jalamedaditi pratItya tasya pratyayasyApAtata evAnyathAtvashaN^kAyAM saMvAdaM niveshya tatsvarUpaprAmANye gR^ihItvA(cha) abhramatvaM nishchitya jalametadbhavatyevetyavadhArya tadupAdatta iti |
nanu nAyamasti niyamo yaduktarItyA.arthatathAtvAdhyavasAyapUrvaka eva vyavahAra iti | tatsandehAdinA.api(dapi) vyavahAradarshanAdityata Aha- sAkShiNa iti ||
vyavasAyI nirashaN^ko.avisaMvA(divya)dI cha vyavahAro.asmAbhiruktarItyA sAkShiNaH kAryo.abhidhIyate na tu vyavahAramAtram.h | nacha vishiShyo vyavahAro.arthatathAtvAdhyavasAyapUrvakatAM vyabhicharatIti | astu vyavahAravilopaH kinnashChinnamityAshaN^kAM pariharannuktAprasaN^gAnAM viparyayaparyavasAnamAha- tasmAditi ||
yasmAtsAkShiNaH kvachidayathArthatve.avishvasanIyatvApattyA kA(ka)raNadoShAdyanishchayaprasaN^gena j~nAnAnAM bhramatvAbhramatvanirdhAraNAbhAvasaktyA.arthatathAtvanirNayAbhAvAnuShaN^geNa nishshaN^ko.avisaMvAdI vyavahAro lupyeta | nacha tallopo.aN^gIkartuM shakyaH | savarlokaprasiddhatvAt.h | tathAvidhasya (cha) laukikaiH parIkShakaishlollaN^ghanAyogAt.h | pramitArthAnanumatAvunmattatvaprasaN^gAt.h | tasmAtsarvalokaprasiddhasya nishshaN^kasyAvisaMvAdino vyavahArasya kAyarbhUtasya siddhaye vastutathAtvAtathAtvanishchayaH kAraNa(karaNI)bhUto.aN^gIkAryaH | tatsiddhaye kA(ka)raNadoShAdinishchayadvArA sAkShiNA j~nAnAnAM bhramatvAbhramatvanirrayo.aN^gIkAryaH | tatsiddhaye (cha) sAkShiNo vishvasanIyatvaM tatsiddhaye cha sAkShI sadA nirdoSho yathArtha eva na

|| OM tadguNasAratvAttu tadvayapadeshaH prAj~navat.h OM || yadyevaM jIveshvarayorbheda eva pAramArthiko vyavasthitastadA tattvamasItyAdyadvaitashrutInAmahaM harirityAdismR^itInAM cha kA gatiH | nahi tAsAmanumAnavatsarvathA.aprAmANyaM yuktam.h | apauruSheyatvenAptoktatvena cha tatkAraNAbhAvAdityAshaN^kAparihArAya sUtram.h | tadguNasAratvAttu tadvayapadeshaH prAj~navaditi | tadvayAchaShye- tathA.apIti || 
yadyapi jIvabrahmaNorbheda eva tathA.apyabhedavaditi sambandhaH | tushabdo visheShArthaH | taM cha vakShyAmaH | tatsadR^ishaH paramAtmaguNasadR^ishAH | sAra ityanuvAdena svarUpamiti vyAkhyAnam.h | asya jIvasya | kutaH | muktAvapi kaivalye.apyavashiShyate yataH | abhedavat.h abhedamiva "tatra tasyeva' ityatropasaN^khayeyametat.h | shiShyaprayogAt.h | yadvA.abheda iti tatpratipAdakamupalakShyate | ata eveti sambandhaH | etAH parodAhR^itAH | hIti mukhye bAdhakaM sUchayati |
ata evetyasyaiva vivaraNaM sAdR^ishyeti | sAdR^ishyamevAbhedaH sAdR^ishyAbhedaH | siMho devadatta ityAdivadgauNo.ayaM vyapadesha iti vAkyArthaH | advaitavAdibhiH khalu tattvaMpadayorviruddhasvArthaikadeshatyAgenaikadeshalakShaNayA sAmAnAdhikaraNyamAtraM mukhyamaN^gIkR^itam.h | tato varaM padadvayasya mukhyArthatvamabhyupagamya sAmAnAdhikaraNyamAtrasya gauNatvamabhyupagantum.h | tAtparyaliN^gAni cha tatra tatrAnyathA nItAni |

Isheneti vartate | na kevalamuktanimittatrayaM kinnAmaitannimittadvayaM vishiShyate | ato visheShaNAbhedoktirupapadyate | tatra sthAnaikyenaikyavyapadesho lAkShaNikaH | sthAnagatasyaikasya sthAniShu prayogAt.h | aikamatyanimitte tu prayoge lakShitalakShaNA | viShayaikyAnmatyaikyaM tatashcha matimatAmiti |
kiJNcha yatsAdR^ishyaM sajjIvamAtrasAdhAraNatayoktaM tatsaMsAriNyanabhivyaktaM mukte tu vyaktamiti tadabhiprAyeNApi visheShato.abhedoktiryuktetyAshayavAnAha- sAdR^ishyaM cheti ||
muktasyesheneti vartate | nanu sAdR^iyAdikaM jaDeShvapi vidyate | tatkathaM teShAM "sarvaM khalvidaM brahma' | "bhUtAni viShNurbhuvanAni viShNurvanAni viShNurgirayo dishashcha' ityAdau kvachideva paramAtmaikyavyapadesho na punarjIvatprAchuryeNetyata Aha- jaDAnAmiti ||

rUpANi matsyAdIni | kriyAH sR^iShyayAdyAH | guNA j~nAnAdayaH | savarsha iti pratyekaM sambandhaH | tathAshabdaH samuchchaye | evashabdasya mukhyata ityenAnvayaH | avayavA hastAdyAH | tatsvarUpaikyam.h IshvarasvarUpeNai(pai)kyaM tatpratipAdakaM vAkyamiti yAvat.h | mukhyata eva vyAkhyeyamiti sheShaH | tushabdo jaDavyAvR^ittyarthaH | tathAcha jaDavisheSha evAyaM dR^iShyAnta iti bhAvaH | nachaivaM sAdhyasamatvadoShaH | jIvamAtrAbhedavAdinaM pratyakShasyAdhikaraNasyArabdhatvAditi | kuta etaditi chet.h(na) | tatra bhedadarshane pratyavAyasyoktatvAdityAha- yatheti ||

nanvIshvaradharmANAM bhedAbhedau bhavatAm.h | tathA chAtyantAbhedoktiramukhyeti sautro dR^iShyAnto.asaN^kuchitavR^ittirbhaviShyati | iyaM cha shrutiratyantabhedadarshananindAparA bhavatvityata Aha- nobhayaM cheti ||

sAdhanavichAro.ayamadhyAyaH | vairAgyArthe gatyAdinirUpaNA prathamapAda ityadhyAyapAdapratipAdyaM bhAShya eva sphuTam.h | saN^gatiM tu lAghavAyaikIkR^ityopari vakShyAma ityAshayavAMstR^itIyA(dhyAya)dyapAdAdhikaraNapUvarpakShasiddhAntayuktIH saN^graheNAha- svAbhAviketi ||
sAdhakA iti vakShyamANaM pUrvapakShasyetyatrApi sambaddhayate | pUrvapakShasya siddhAntasyeti jAtAvekavachanam.h | sAdhakA iti ChAndaso nirdeshaH | yadvA yuktayaH pUrvapakShasyetyatra sAdhakA iti nyakR^iShyate | pUrvapakShasambandhino yuktaya ityevArthaH | siddhAntasyaiva sAdhakA ityatra tu nyAyA iti sheShaH | 
atra sUtram.h yoneH sharIramiti | tadvayAkhyAtaM bhAShye | svargAdavAggato jIvo vR^iShyidvArA vrIhyAdibIjeShu saN^krAnto retasmi(chaMpu)k.hpuruShaM pravishya saha retasA mAtR^iyonidvAreNa jaTharaM praviShyaH kalalabR^idbudAdikrameNotpannaM sharIramApnotIti prasiddham.h | tatkiM tathyamutAtathyamiti sandehaH | na tathyamiti pUrvaH pakShaH | kutaH | "dehaM garbhasthitaM kvApi pravishetsvargato gataH' ityAdivachanAt.h | mAndhAtR^idroNadrupadakR^ipAkAdInAmitihAsapurANeShu vinaiva bIjAdisambandhena jananadarshanAchcha | anyathAsiddhe chAthare na bahukalpanA yuktA | ataste vairAgyajanakA(yaivA)rthamevAdhyAtmavidAM vAdAH' iti | tathyamiti siddhAntaH | kasmAt.h | "memegho bhUtvA varShati | ta(dya) iha vrIhiyavA oSha(dhivanaspataya)dhayastilAmAShA iti jAyante | yo yo hyannamatti | yo vA retaH siJNchati tadrUpAdbhUya eva bhavati | tadya iha ramaNIyacharaNA abhyAsho ha yatte ramaNIyAM yonimApadyante' ityAdishruteH | na chAdR^iShye.arthenyathAsiddhiravakAshavatI | nacha vachanAntaraliN^gadasharnavirodhaH | kvachid.h bIjAdisambandhAbhAvasyApi vidyAmAnatvena tadviShayatvAt.h | yathoktam.h | "divaH sthAsnUn.h gachChati' | "sthAvarANi divaH prAptaH' iti shrutismR^itibhyAmiti |
tadidamayuktaM vyAkhyAnam.h | utsUtratvAt.h | yadyapyatra yonishabdo bIjAdyupalakShaNaH shakyo vyAkhyAtuM tathA.api tatsambandhaniyama eva sUtre pratIyate | natu kvAchitkastadabhAvo.api | yadi cha kvachid.h bIjAdisambandhAbhAvaH syAttadA.a.akasmikatvaM syAdityata Aha- bIjeti ||
bIjashabdena vrIhyAdikaM retashchochyate | saN^gatiniyamojkhitiM sambandhAtiniyamAbhAvam.h | ayamarthaH | retaHsiNyogo.atheti pUrvasUtrAdathashabdo.atrApyanuvartate | sa cha prakR^itAdarthAdarthAntare vartate | tathAcha yoneH sharIramApadyate | kvachittadabhAvenApItyathashabdena bhagavAnsUtrakAro bIjAdisamba(ndhe ni)ndhaniyamAbhAvaM sUtritavAnityato notsUtratvaparyanuyogo yukta iti | 
yaduktamevaM satyAkasmikatvaprasaN^ga iti tatpariharati- kAraNatashcheti ||
tAM cha bIjAdisambandhaniyamojkhitiM kAraNAt.h Aha | etaduktaM bhavati | janmakAraNAdR^iShyAkR^iShyo janturbIjAdisambandhena sharIramApadyata ityutsargaH | sa cha kvachijj~nAnatapoyogAdyatishayalakShaNena kAraNavisheShaNApodyate | yathA kShudrajantuyAtanAsharIrotpattAvapavAda iti | tathA choktam.h | "visheShakAraNAdeva visheShAjjaniriShyate | sAmAnyajananaM chaiva nR^iNAM 
sAmAnyahetutaH' iti | ato yuktametadvayAkhyAnamiti | 
|| iti shrImatpUrNapramatibhagavatpAdasukR^iteranuvyAkhyAnasya praguNajayatIrthAkhyayatinA | kR^itAyAM TIkAyAM viShamapadavAkyArthavivR^itau tR^itIye.adhyAye.ayaM prathamacharaNaH paryavasitaH | 
"bhaktirasminpAda uchyate | bhaktyarthaM hi bhagavanmahimoktiH' iti pAdApratipAdyaM bhAShya eva sphuTam.h | saN^gatiM tUttaratra vakShyAma ityAshayavAnetatpAdAdhikaraNe pUrvapakShasiddhAntayuktIH saN^graheNAha- pashchAditi ||
pUrvapakShagAH pUrvapakShasambandhinyaH | nirNayapramAH siddhAntanirNayArthAni pramANAni | 
|| OM sandhye sR^iShyirAha hi OM || yoneH sharIramityetadavasAnaiH sUtrairjIvasya janmAvagatam.h | jAtasya cha svapanAdyavasthAsambandhaH prasiddhaH | tatra svapnAvasthApravartakatvalakShaNo mahimAbhagavato.atrAdhikaraNe nirNIyate | tathAhi | svapno nAmArthaj~nAnAtmakaH | tatra tAvatsvApnArthAnAM karituragAdInAM parameshvarAyattatA nopapadyate | asatyatvAt.h | na tAvadime.anAdinityAH | svapnAvasthAtaH prAgUrdhvaM chopalabdhiprasaN^gAt.h | nahi vidyamAnA apyupalabdhisAdhaneShu chakShurAdiShvanuparateShu nopalabhyante, upalabhyante chopapatteriti sambhavati | nachAnyatra gatAH | anyairapyanupalambhAt.h | madyamaparimANashchaite dR^ishyante | nacha tathAvidhamanAdinityaM kimapi dR^iShyam.h | nApyutpattinAshavantaH | tathAtve.api prAgUrdhvamupalambhaprasakteH | nacha vAchyaM vidyudAdivattadaivotpattirvinAshashcheti | itthambhAve pramANAbhAvAt.h | prAD.hmR^idAdInAmUrdhvaM kapAlAdInAM chopalambhApatteshcha | nachaiteShAM (tAtkAlika)tatkAlInajanmanyupAdAnaM nimittaM cha pashyAmaH | kartA cha na tAvajjIvAtmA | draShyurnivyarApAratvAt.h | aparasya chAdarshanAt.h | nApIshvaraH | pramANAbhAvAt.h | bhrAntitvaM chaiteShAm.h, "svApnamAyAsarUpaH' iti "svApnamanoratho yathA' ityAdishrutismR^itibhyAmAvedyate | shiShyamapavyAkhyAnAnuvAde vakShyAmaH | tadevaM na svApnAnAmarthAnAmIshvarAdhInatvam.h | nApi tajj~nAnasya | tasyApi nimittAbhAvenAparamArthatvAt.h | natAvachchakShurAdInAM ta(tra nimi)nnimittatvam.h | teShAmuparatatvAt.h | nApi manasaH | rUpAdimatyarthe sAmarthyAbhAvAt.h (svAtantAbhAvAt.h) | ata eva na sAkShiNaH | sa indriyApravR^ittau liN^gashabdayorapi nAvakAshaH | aparokShAkAraM chedamavabhAsate | ato.arthaj~nAnarUpA svApnAvasthA neshvarAdhIneti prApte tatpratividhAnAyopodghAtamAha- vAsanA iti ||
bhAvanA.aparanAmakAH saMskArAH | sarvagrahaNaprayojanamuttaratra bhaviShyati | nanu bhAvanAkhyasaMskAro.anubhavajanyaH | nacha sarvajIvAnAM sarvavastvanubhavo.asti | tatkathamasheShajIvAnAM sarvavastuvAsanAH santyevetyata uktam.h- anAdIti || anAdyanubhavapravAhotpannAH | vAsanAnAmAtmasamavetatvaM vaisheShikAdibhirabhyupagatam.h | tannirAsArthamuktaM manasi sthitA iti | jAtAvekavachanam.h | sAdito manasaH kathamanAdivAsanAsambandha ityata uktam.h- anAdIti || 
etadeva prapaJNchayati- triguNAtmakamiti ||
manasa eva saMskArAshrayatvaM nAtmana itayatropapattisUchanAya triguNAtmakamityuktam.h | guNAtmakamityevokte parimANAdiguNAtmakamityapi pratItiH syAt.h | tadAtmano.api samAnamityatastrigrahaNam.h | tathAcha jIvAtmA na bhAvanAshrayaH sattvAdiguNAnAtmakatvAdIshvaravat.h | bhAvanA vA sattvAdiguNAtmakadravyAshrayA saMskAratvAdvegAdivat.h | tachcha parisheShAnmana evetyuktaM bhavati | sattvAdiguNAnabhyupagantAraM prati tu tatsthAne.achetanapadaM prayoktavyam.h | triguNAtmakagrahaNaM (cha)svarUpakathanam.h | astyeva sarva(daiveti)deti sheShaH | tathA sati mokShe.api sattvAtsvapnAdyavasthApattirityata uktaM vivR^iNoti- yAvaditi || yadyapi manaH svarUpeNa nityameva tathA.api jIvasambandhastasya mokShAvadhirityata idamuktam.h | (tadvai devaM) tadvai jaivaM mano yenAnandyeta bhavatIti sUktAvapyAtmano manaHsambandhashravaNAtkathaM yAvanmuktirityuktamityato vA triguNAtmakamityuktam.h | AtmasvarUpamanaso muktau sattve.api jaDamano.abhipretyAyamavadhirukta iti | chastasmAdityarthe | tatraiva na tvAtmani | 
"etasmAjjAyate prANo manaH sarvendriyANi cha' iti manaso janmashravaNAtkathamanAditvamuchyata ityata Aha- sUkShmatveneti ||
chashabda evArthe | prAkR^itaiH ahaN^kArAdyaiH | mana iti vartate | pralaye sato.apyupachayApekShayA janmashrutiriti bhAvaH | kuta eShA kalpanA | mukhyArthe bAdhakasadbhAvAdityAha- yadeti || yadi mano mukhyata eva janimatsyAttadA pralaye tanna syAt.h | yadi cha pralaye tanna syAttadA.a.atmanaH saMsArAvasthAnaM na syAt.h | nacha mA bhUtpralaye saMsArAvasthAnamiti yuktam.h | muktAnAM punaH saMsArAnupapattyA sR^iShyayanupapattiprasaN^gAt.h | avidyAkAmakarmAdyadhInaH saMsAra iti chenna | avidyAdereva saMsAratvAt.h, "manaH paraM kAraNamAmananti' ityAdismR^itivirodhAchcha | tathAcha shrutiH | "nityaM mano.anAditvAnna hyamanAH pumAMstiShThati' iti | pumAnsaMsArItyarthaH | 
kimato yadyevaM sarvavastvanubhavAhitasaMskArasadbhAva ityata Aha- saMskArairiti || 
atra sR^iShTvetyanenAnAdinityatvapakShadoShA anabhyupagamenaiva nirastAH | svapnakAla eva sR^iShTvetyanena prAgUrdhvaM chopalambhaprasaN^go nirAkR^itaH | sR^iShyeH saMhAropalakShaNatvAt.h | saMskArairityupAdAnakIrtanam.h | nacha teShAM guNatvenopAdAnatvAnupapattiH | manovR^ittitvena dravyatvAt.h | saMskArANAM chAtIndriyatvena tyaNukajanmavinAshayoriva prAgUrdhvaM chAnupalambho na doShAya | bhagavAniti kartR^inirdeshaH | tadaiva sR^iShyisaMhArakaraNamasambhAvitamityato.ashakyakartR^itAshaktisUchanAya bhagavAnityuktam.h | evaM cha satyadR^iShyAdinimittaM prasiddhameva | na kevalamarthAnAM satyatvasambhavena bhagavadadhInatvam.h, api tu tajj~nAnasyApItyuktaM darshayatIti | jIvAyeti sheShaH | darshanasAdhanaM cha mana eveti vakShyati | darshanaM chAnubhavo vivakShitaH | tena smaraNamevaitaditi mataM nirastaM bhavati |
smaraNatvaM khalvasya tachchihnasya tadityullekhasya sadbhAvAdvA kalpyate | asannihitagocharatvAdvA saMskAraprabhavatvAdvA | nAdyaH | idamityullekhena tadabhAvAt.h | ata eva smR^itiviparyAso.ayamiti chenna | smR^ititvasyaivAsiddheH | na dvitIyaH | viShayasAnnidhyasyopapAditatvAt.h | na tR^itIyaH | padArthajanmani saMskArasyopakShINatvenAsiddheH | tasmAdyathA manorathe dhyAne vA saMskArayonInarthAnmanasA.anubhavatyevaM svapne.apIti kimanupapannam.h | iyAMstu visheShaH | manorathAdau prayatnapUrvikA padArthasR^iShyiH | svapne punarIshva(rechChAdhI)rAdhInaiveti |
apare tu bhavatyevAyamanubhavaH | kintu jAgarAnubhUtasmartavyArtha eveti manyante | tadapyasat.h | tathAhi | kimayamanubhavo yathArtha utAyathArthaH | nAdyaH | bAhyAtharAnAM deshakAlaviprakR^iShyatvena tadanupapatteH | dvitIye vaktavyaM kimayamagaje gajatvollekhItyayamayathArthaH, kiMvA gaja evAsannikR^iShye sannikR^iShyatvollekhItyayathArthaH | Adye nAyaM gajaH kintu gavaya eveti bAdodayaH syAt.h | dvitIye nAyaM sannikR^iShyaH kinnAma viprakR^iShya iti bAdho bhavet.h | na chaitadasti | tasmAtsaMskAraprabhavasannikR^iShyasatyArthapramitireveyamiti yuktam.h | kathaM tarhi shrutismR^itiShu svapnapratIterbhrAntitvamuchyata ityata Aha- bhrAntiriti ||
jAgrattvamiti tatpratItimupalakShayati | eveti padArthasvarUpaM vyAvartayati | jAgrattvaM jAgarAnubhUtapadArthairekatvam.h | svapne hi tAtkAlikatayA.adR^iShyacharAneva tanayAdIndR^iShyacharatayA.anusandhatte | yadvA jAgrattvaM nAma gaganAdInAM nityatvAdikam.h | ghaTAdInAM mR^idAdyupAdAnakatvaM bAhyArthakriyAkShamatvamityAdi grAhyam.h | jAgrattvapratIterbhrAntitvAttadviShayaM shrutyAdikamiti bhAvaH | 
syAdetat.h | jAgrattvasyApi saMskAro.astyeveti sopAdAnatvasambhavAtkathaM tatpratItiH bhrAntirityuchyate | anyathA.arthapratItirapi bhrAntiH syAdavisheShAditi | maivam.h | nahi vayaM kAraNasAmagrIsambhavamAtreNArthAnAM satyatAmAtiShThAmahe | kintu bAdhAbhAveneti vakShyAmaH | sAmagyrabhAvenAsatyatvaM bruvANaM prati tu tadasiddhi(rA)revAveditA | asti cha jAgrattA(ttva)pratIterbAdhaH | svApna evAyaM na jAgarAnubhUta ityAdyudayAt.h | tadidamuktaM hishabdena | 
jAgrattvrapratItireva bhrAntirityayuktam.h | arthAnAmapi keShAJNchidasattvena tatpratIterapi bhrAntitvAt.h | svapne.api svashirachChedAdayo.api pratIyante | nacha tadutpattAvupAdAnamasti | ananubhUtatvena saMskArodayAyogAt.h | ananubhUte.api saMskArodayAbhyupagame "adR^iShye chAshruteH' ityAdishrutismR^itivirodhaH syAt.h | kadAchidananubhUtArthasmR^itirapyApadyeta | tato yadyapi sAkShAtsvashirachChedAdebarAdho nAsti tathA.api kAraNAnupapattyA.asattvamaN^gIkAryamevetyata Aha- adR^iShye cheti || 
bhAve padArthe | bhAvo vAsanA | paJNchamI saptamyarthe | uktirityataH parastushabdo boddhavyaH | anAditvAt.h saMsArasyeti sheShaH | saMsArasyAnAditvAtkvachijjanmani svashirashchChedAderapyanubhavasambhavena saMskAropapatteH | satyatve.api shrutipurANoktiryujyata eva, na tu viruddhayate | vinApyanubhavena saMskArodayAbhyupagame hi sA viruddhayeteti | atrAshrutagrahaNenAtrApi janmani shravaNajanitasaMskAraH sambhavatIti sUchyate | yatra tu shravaNAdyapi nAsti tatrAnAditvaM niveshitam.h | anena yatpUrvaM sarvagrahaNaM kR^itaM tadupapattaye vA.anAdyanubhavaparamparoktA tasya sarvasyopayogaH kathito bhavati |
nanu (cha) shashaviShANAdipratItau katham.h | nahi bhavAntare.api tadanubhavaH sambhavati | yathApUrvamiti sarvakalpAnAmekavidhatvashravaNAt.h | maivam.h | shashaviShANAdipramAbhAve.api shabdAdinA bhrAntisambhavena saMskAropapatteH | yena tu shashaviShANAdikaM bhrAntyA.api na pratipannaM tasya katham.h | nahi (savo.api) sarvatra bhrAmyatIti niyamo.asti | nApi svapne na tatpashyatIti niyantuM shakyate | uchyate | kimatra shashAdInAM viShANAdInAM chopAdAnAsambhavenAsattvamuchyate | uta shashatvAdiviShANitvAdisAmAnAdhikaraNyAdeH | 
AdyaM nirAkaroti- kadAchiditi || 
yatsvapne dR^ishyata iti sheShaH | vibhAgataH sAmAnAdhiraNyena vinA dR^iShyaM jAgare | yadyapi shashatvaviShANitvAdInAM sAmAnAdhikaraNyaM shashaviShANAdisambandhavisheSho vA jAgare nAnubhUtastathA.api viviktaM shashatvAdikamanubhUtameveti tatsaMskArasambhave(na) na shashAdInAmasattvaM vAchyamiti | 
dvitIye sampratipattimuttaramAha- sameti ||
bhAvapradhAno nirdeshaH | upalakShaNaM chaitat.h | dR^ishyata ityatra prakR^ityarthaM sa iti parAmR^ishati | yadityanuvartate | atra svapne na kevalaM jAgrattvamiti chArthaH | yasyopAdAnaM sambhavati bAdhashcha nAsti | tadeva hi prAgevashabdena vyavachChinnamiti bhAvaH | 
bhavedetatsarvaM yadi svApnArthAnAM jAgaropalabdhAnAmiva spaShyatayA bAhyArthakriyAsAmarthyalakShaNA nAsti | anyathA sA syAdityarthaH | 
ayamabhisandhiH | svApnAstAvadghaTAdayo nAsanto bAdhAbhAvAt.h | nApyanAdinityAH | pUrvottaramanupalambhAt.h | na(cha)nirupAdAnotpattirupapannA | tato.avashyamupAdAne.anusaraNIye | na tAvadbAhya(tte bAhya)mR^idAdyupAdAnAH | bAhyArthakriyAsAmarthyarahitatvAt.h | vimato ghaTo na bAhyamR^idAdyupAdAnako bAhyamR^idAdyupAdAnako bAhyamR^idAdyupAdAnakAryakriyArahitatvAt.h (paTavat.h) iti prayogAt.h | anyathA tatprasaN^gAt.h | nachopAdAnAntaramasti | tataH parisheShAdvAsanopAdAnakA eveti | chashabdena bhagavatkartR^ikatve tAtkAlikotpattivinAshitve cha parisheSham.h "ya eSha supteShu jAgarti' "etasmAddhayeva putro jAyate' "na tatra rathAH' ityAdishrutiM cha pramANaM samuchchinoti | 
tadanena prabandhena sandhye sR^iShyirAha hi | nirmAtAraM chaike putrAdayashcha | mAyAmAtraM tu kAtsnaryenAnabhivyaktasvarUpatvAditi trisUtrI vyAkhyAtA bhavati |
anye punaranyathaitAni sUtrANi vyAchakShate | 
tathAhi | "na tatra rathA na rathayogA na panthAno bhavantyatha rathAn.hrathayogAnpathaH sR^ijate' ityAdi shrUyate | tatra saMshayaH | kiM prabodha iva svapne.api pAramArthikI sR^iShyirAhosvinmAyAmayIti | tatra tAvatpratipadyante | sandhye sR^iShyirAha hi | prabodha (svApasthAna) samprasAda(yoH saM) sthAnayoH sandhau, bhavatIti sandhyaM svApnasthAnam.h | tatra tathArUpaiva sR^iShyiH | kutaH | yataH pramANabhUtA shrutirevamAha | "atha rathAn.hrathayogAnpathaH sR^ijate' ityAdi | 
nirmAtAraM chaike putrAdayashcha | api chaike shAkhinaH sandhye kAmAnAM nirmAtAramAtmAnamAmananti | "ya eSha supteShu jAgarti kAmaM kAmaM puruSho nirmimANaH' iti | putrAdayashcha tatra kAmA abhipreyante kAmyanta iti, na punarichChAvisheShAH | "shatAyuShaH putrapautrAnvR^iNIShva' iti prakR^iteShu putrAdiShu "kAmAnAM tvA kAmabhAjaM karomi' iti kAmashabdasya prayuktatvAt.h | 
prAj~naM chainaM nirmAtAraM prakaraNavAkyasheShAbhyAM pratImaH | "anyatra dharmAdanyatrAdharmAt.h' ityAdeH prAj~nasya hIdaM prakaraNam.h | vAkyasheSho.api "tadeva shukraM tadbrahma' ityAdiH | prAj~nakartR^ikA cha sR^iShyi(stathAbhUtA)ryathArUpA sandhye sR^iShyiriti |
evaM prApte pratyAha- mAyAmAtraM tu kAtsnaryenAnabhivyaktasvarUpatvAt.h | tushabdaH pakShaM vyAvartayati | mAyetyanAdiranirvAchyA.avidyochyate | mAyaiva sandhye sR^iShyirna paramArthagandho.apyasti | kutaH | mAyetyanAdiranirvAchy.avidyochyate | mAyaiva sandhye sR^iShyirna paramArthagandho.apyasti | kutaH | kAtsnaryenAnabhivyaktasvarUpatvAt.h | deshakAlanimittasampattirabAdhashcha kAtsnaryaM tenAbhivyaktasvarUpatvAbhAvAt.h |
tathAhi | na tAvatsvapne rathAdInAmuchito deshaH sambhavati | nahi saMvR^ite dehadeshe rathAdayo.avakAshaM labheran.h | nacha vAchyaM "bahiH kulAyAdamR^itashcharitvA' iti shruteH sthitigatipratyayabhedAchcha bahirdehAtsvapnaM pashyatIti | suptasya jantoryojanashatAntaritaM deshaM kShaNamAtreNa paryetuM viparyetu cha tataH (sarvataH)sAmarthyA(bhAvA)sambhavAt.h | kvachichcha pratyAgamanavarjitaH svapno bhavati | kuruShvahamadya shayAnaH svapne pAJNchAlAnadhigatashcha pratibuddhashcheti | dehAchchedapeyAtpAJNchAleShu pratibudhyeta | kuruShveva tu pratibudhyate | yena chAyaM dehena deshAntarANi svapne pashyati, na tAni tathAbhUtAnyeva bhavanti | paridhAvaMshchetpashyejjAgradvad.hbhUtamarthamAkalayet.h | darshayati cha shrutirantareva svapnaM "sve sharIre yathAkAmaM parivartate' iti | atashcha shrutyupapattiviredhAdbahiH shrutiranupakAritvasAmyAdgauNI vyAkhyeyA | sthitigatipratyayabhedashcha bhrAnto.abhyupeyaH | 
kAlavisaMvAdo.api svapne bhavati | rajanyAM supto hi vAsaraM bhArate varShe manyante | tathA muhUrtamAtramapi varSham.h | nimittAnyapi (cha) svapne na buddhaye karmaNe vochi(chochi)tAni vidyante | bAdhyante chaite rathAdayaH svapne dR^iShyAH prabodhe | svapne eva chaite sulabhabAdhA bhavanti | AdyantayorvyabhichAradarshanAt.h | ratho.ayamiti hi kadAchitsvapne nirdhAritaH kShaNena manuShyaH sampadyate | manuShyo.ayamiti nirdhAritaH kShaNena vR^ikShaH | 
spaShyaM chAbhAvaM rathAdInAM svapne shrAvayati shAstram.h | "na tatra rathA na rathayogA na panthAno bhavanti' ityAdi | tasmAnmAyAmAtraM svapanadarshanam.h | 
apara Aha kAtsnaryenAnabhivyaktasvarapUtvAd.h draShyubhirnnatvAdinA nirvaktumashakyatvAt.h | tathAhi | svApnAnAM rathAdInAM draShyurbhedo.abhedo bhedAbhedo vA | na tAvadbhedaH | pAshvarsthAnAmapi tadupalambhaprasaN^gAt.h | Antaratvasya chAnuchitatvAt.h | nApyabhedaH | ekasyAvichitrasya vichitrAnekAtmakatAyA vinA bhrAntimanupapatteH | bhedapratyayavirodhAchcha | nacha bhedAbhedau | vyAghAtAt.h | ato.anirvAchyAvidyAlAsa evAyamiti |
sUchakashcha hi shruterAchakShate cha tadvidaH | mAyAmAtratvAttarhi na kashchitsvapne paramArthagandha iti netyuchyate | sUchakashcha hi svapno bhavati bhaviShyatoH sAdhvasAdhunoH | kutaH | yadA karmasvityAdishruteH | AchakShate cha svapnAdhyAyavidaH | tatra bhavatu sUchyamAnasya satyatvam.h | sUchakasya tu vaitathyameveti bhAvaH | 
yaduktam.h "Aha hi' iti | tadevaM sati bhAktaM vyAkhyeyam.h | suptau hi svapnadarshananimittasukR^itaduShkR^itakartR^itvAdrathAdInAM kartetyuchyate | nirmANashrutirapyevaM bhAktA vyAkhyeyA | 
yadapyuktaM prAj~namenaM nirmAtAramAmanantIti tadapyasat.h | shrutyantare "svayaM vihR^itya svayaM nirmAya' iti jIvavyApArashravaNAt.h | 
aparastvetadarthameva sUchakashcheti sUtraM vyAkhyAtavAn.h | shubhAshubhasUchako hi svapnaH | nahi prAj~nasya shubhAshubhayogo.avakalpata iti | jIvasyaiva tadeva shuklamiti vAkyasheShe jIvabhAvaM vyAvartya brahmabhAva upadishyate tattvamasItyAdivaditi na brahmaprakaraNaM viruddhaya(to)te | astu vA svapne.api prAj~navyavahAraH | na(cha) tAvatA viyadAdivatsvapnasya satyatvam.h | vaiShamyasyoktatvAt.h | viyadAdiprapaJNcho.apyasatya evetyupapAditaM chArambhaNAdhikaraNe | brahmAtmatvadarshanAdviyadAdiprapaJNcho bAdhyate | sandhyAshrayastu pratidinamityato vaisheShikamidaM sandhyasya mAyAmAtratvamu(papA)ditam.h | 
parAbhidhyAnAttu tirohitaM tato hyasya bandhaviparyayau | nanyagneraMshasya viShphuliN^gasya yathA dahanaprakAshanashaktI bhavatastatheshvarAMshasya jIvasyApi j~nAnaishvaryashaktibhyAM bhAvyam.h | tatashcha sAN^kalpikI sR^iShyiH syAdityasyedamuttaram.h | satyamastyeveshvarasAdharmyaM jIvasya kintu tirohitam.h | tattu parameshvarAbhidhyAnAdevAvirbhavati | kutaH | tato hIshvarAddhetorasya jIvasya bandhamokShau bhavataH | dehayogAdvA so.api | kasmAjjIvasya j~nAnaishvaryatiraskAro bhavati | viShphuliN^gavadatiraskAro hi yukta ityatredamuttaram.h | so.api tiraskAro jIvasya dehayogAt.h | avidyApratyupasthApitanAmarUpakR^itadehendriyamanobuddhiviShayavedanAdyupAdhiyogAttadavivekabhramakR^ito bhavati | yathA.araNiyogAdagneH | kimanayA kalpanayA | anya evAstu jIvaH parameshvarAdityetadvAshabdena | vyavachChinatti | maivam.h | tattvamasyAdishrutivirodhAditi |
tadidamanupapannaM vyAkhyAnam.h | tathAhi | yattAtsvapnasR^iShyeH pAramArthikatvapratipAdakaM sUtradvayaM pUrvapInuvAdaparamiti tattadA pratImo yadi mAyAmAtramityanirvAchyatvapratij~nA syAt.h | nachaivam.h | tatpratipAdakapramANAbhAvAt.h | 
nanUktaM kAtsnaryenAnabhivyaktasvarUpatvAditi deshakAlanimittasampattyabAdharAhityaM tathA bhinnatvAdinA nirUpayitumashakyatvaM cha | maivam.h | tasyAnupapannatvAt.h | tatra yaddeshAdirAhityamupapAditam.h | tatsUtrArthaspaShyIkaraNenaivAbhAsIbhaviShyatItyAshayavAn.h bhedAdivikalpaprashnena yat.h dUShaNamuktaM tatra prashna evAsAvanupapanno dUre dUShaNAbhidhAnamityAha- bheda iti ||
draShyurdevadattAtsvapnasya svapnopalabhyasya rathAdeH kiM bhedo.athAbhedo dvandvaM bhedAbhedau veti vikalpa(lpya) prashno na yujyate | 
kuta ityata Aha- dR^iShyatvAditi ||
draShyuH svapnasyetyanuvartate | sandehamUlo hi vikalpaprashnaH | nacha prakR^ite sandehaH sambhavati | svapnataddraShyrorbhedasyaivAkhilairjanairdR^iShyatvena vipratipatterabhAvAt.h |
syAdetat.h | mA bhUdvipratipattimUlo.ayaM saMshayaH | samAnadharmajastu bhaviShyati | kiJNchidvastu draShyurbhinnaM bhavati kiJNchidabhinnaM kiJNchidbhinnAbhinnam.h | vastu chedamato bhinnamabhinnaM vetyAdisaMshayo bhavediti | maivam.h | saMshayo hi kiM samAnadharmadarshanamAtrAdbhavati | uta nirNAyakAbhAvasahakR^itAt.h | nAdyaH | sarvatra sandehotpAdaprasaN^gAt.h | asti hi sarvatra kiJNchit.h sAdharmyam.h | tadanivR^ittiprasaN^gAchcha | nahi samAno dharmaH kadA.api nivartate | dvitIye tu kathamatra sandehaH | bhedasyaivAkhilairjanairdR^iShyatvena nirNAyakAbhAvasyaivAsiddheH | 
atha matam.h | bhedo hi kashchitparamArtho dR^iShyo yathA stambhakumbhayoH | kashchi(chchApa)daparamArtho yathA chandramasoH | dR^ishyate chAyaM 
bhedastato bhavedeva sandeha iti | etadapi na | tathA sati yathAsaMshayaM vikalpaprashnasya kAryatvAt.h | sa evAnayA vAchobhaN^gayA kriyata iti chenna | pratItirapi hi na kevalA saMshayaheturbhavati | sarvatra (saMshaya)prasaN^gAt.h | tadanivR^ittiprasaN^gAchcha | visheShapratItyA hi tannivR^ittireShyavyA | tatrApi cha sandeho.avaskandata eva | kintu vipratipattyAdikaluShitA | nachAtra tadastItyuktam.h | autsargikaM hi pratItInAM yAthAthyarm.h | anyathAtvaM tvapavAdam.h | tadevaM siddhaviShayatvAtprashna evAyamanupapannaH | 
nanu cha bhedapakShamevAN^gIkR^itya tatrokto doShaH shakyata eva parihartum.h | manoyonitvena sukhAdivatpArshvasthAnupalambhasambhavAt.h | tatkimanena prashnakhaNDena | satyam.h | tathA.api prativAdissvakhilaM nopekShAmarhatIti shiShyAMchChikShayitumetat.h | tathAcha vakShyati | yuktipAdavyutpAditanyAyasheShaM prasaN^gena vyutpAdayituM cha | iha cha tad.hvyutpAdanasyopayogaM leshato darshayiShyAmaH | 
siddhe.arthe saMshayo na yujyate | tato vikalpaprashno.apItyuktam.h | tatra na yujyata iti ko.arthaH | na tAvannotpadyata iti | saMshayavikalpaprashnotpatteH pramitatvAt.h | na chotpanno.api niShkAraNa iti | akAraNakAryotpatteH pramANaviruddhatvAt.h | nApyatatkAraNAdutpanna iti | yata utpannastasyaiva kAraNatvena vyAhatatvAt.h | nachAnyadanupapannatvamastItyata Aha- prashneti ||
vikalpaprashnadoShAHDha | pramANavyAhatiH siddhArthataiveti na pR^ithaguktaH | svavyAhatiryathA | vandhyA kiM putravatI na veti | asaN^gatiryathA | IshvaraH sukhItyukte prapaJNchasya kShaNikatve kiM pratyakShaM pramANamutAnumitiriti | siddhArthasya tu prakR^itaiva | vaiphalatyaM yathA | kAkasyAShyau dasha vA dantA iti | vaiphalyamityataHparamitishabdo.adhyAhAyarH | 
ayamabhisandhiH | svavyAhatyAdikaM tAvattrayaM prashnadUShaNaM bhavatyeva | pratij~nAvirodArthAntarAdernigrahasthAnatvena prAmANikaiH parigaNitatvAt.h | tasyAnupapannatA kIdR^ishI yena dUShaNatvamiti vaktavyam.h | 
atha manyeta | avyA(ghAtAdi)hatyAdikamarthapratyayanAN^gam.h | vyAhatAdikaM cha bruvANastanna pratyeti viparItaM cha pratyetItyanumIyate | ato.apratipattivipratipattiliN^gatvAdanupapannamiti | evaM tarhi siddhArthatA.apyevameveti kathaM na doShaH | vikalpaprashno hi sandehamUlaH | sandehashcha samAnadharmadarshanAdinA nirNAyakAbhAvasahakR^itena bhavati | samAnadharmAdyabhAve vA nirNAyakasadbhAve.api vA yaH sandigdhe vikalpAMshcha pR^ichChati sa nUnamavidyAmAnameva samAnadharmAdikaM pratipanno na pratipannashcha nirNAyakasadbhAvamityanumIyate | nacha kAryamakAraNaM bhavitumarhati | dR^ishyate hi sarpabhramAdinA.api bhayakampAdikAryotpAda iti | 
nanu granthAstAvadime vAdakathAprakriyayA pravR^ittAH | nacha vAde nigrahasthAnamasti | tasya tattvanirNayAvasAnatvAt.h | nahi vAdiprativAdinoranyarasminpratij~nAhAnyAdinA nigR^ihIte satyantarapakShanirNayaH siddhayati | punaH samyak.h pratipAdya pratyavasthAnasambhavAt.h | yattu vAdasUtre "siddhAntAviruddhaH paJNchAvayavopapannaH' ityapasiddhAntAdernigrahasthAnatvaM sUchitam.h | tadapi vAdasyAnyatarapakShaniNaryAvasAnatvavirodhAdanupapannam.h | yadi cha vAde.apasiddhAntAdIni kAnichinnigrahasthAnAni syustadAparaNyapi kasmAnna syuH | tattvanirNayAvasAnatvaviro(dhitvasyo)dhasyobhayatra sAmyAt.h | pratij~nAhAnyAdinA nigrahe vItarAgatvahA(niriti)niH syAditi chet.h | samamapasiddhAntadAvapIti | ato vAde nigrahasthAnAbhAvAtkathaM prashnadoShodbhavanamityata Aha- na tairiti || 
taiH svavyAhatAdiprashnaiH | svavyAhatAdiprashnAstattvanirNayavirodhina ityarthaH | nahi siddhe.apyarthe sandihAnaH shatenApi pramANAnAM tattvaM pratipAdayituM shakyate | (tatra) tatrApi sandehAnivAraNAt.h | JOSHI-12
